L’orthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser
pour savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous
ne voyez pas ici sont les mêmes qu'en
français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x n'existent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début d'un
mot.
Voici le reste de l'alphabet :

5

"Nimlʋʋ : 29 "Su : -Zroo -Kwɛ : 2009

"Su -bha 'sëëdhɛ -mü		"Gwɛɛtaawo	

‘Wɔn yaa kë –sü =ya sɔ =dɛɛ -dedewo

‘Në dhebë ‘në ya, -a -kwɛ -yö kaɔng do ö ga do ‘yö dho ö dhuëë- =keng- ‘yö- dhuëë bha ‘ö ‘gu dɔ- -bha.

﻿
<h>“Dhi -wo -yan kpö ‘në ‘ö go ‘sëëdhɛ ya, -a -bɛn zë -mɛ “piʋ̈</h>

‘Sëëdhɛ ya -yö -dho ‘pö- -mɛ -nu =në- -nu “piʋ̈ kpɛnngdhö. -A -gɛn -mü =dhɛ -a -nu ‘gbɛ -dhɛ ‘waa =dhɔtrɔɔ =plöödhɛ “sɔɔ.

Yö =në- -wɔn ‘gü, ‘yö -kɔ ‘ö ‘wo dho wo “dhɛ kë- ‘ka- -bha, ‘yö ‘sëëdhɛ ya ‘ö- -a sɛɛnnë ‘bha pö.

-A -bɛn ‘yaa zë -sü ‘ka -wo kpö “gblʋ̈gblʋ̈ ‘gü.

=Ya ‘go mü, ‘pë nu ‘ö- -nu bhawɔn ‘dhö nu bha kö -wa nu kë, kö kë “klʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ sü yö kë -a -nu gɔ kpɛawo, ‘yö a nu dhiang zë. A wɔn ‘gü, yö së -a -nu bha ‘ka kö wa wo pö. A ‘gü wɔn nu wo mɔɔ a -bha ‘ö ‘wo- dha “iin ‘ö ‘wo -a -nu -bha mɛ ‘bha dha.=Bɛdhɛ nu ‘ö a nu ‘tɔ nu ‘wo ‘sëëdhɛ ya ‘gü, dhioo wo nu ‘ö ‘wo ‘gü, ‘mɛ nu ‘ö waa nu blɛɛsü nu kë, “iin ‘ö waa nu ya =blëë ‘gü, ‘mɛ ‘kö yöö pö a nu bha wo ya, a mɛ ‘yaa ‘dhö. A nu bha kë tiaandhö sü ‘ö bha, ‘yaa za -dɔ ‘gü wɔn ‘ka ‘zü.




﻿
<h>1) ‘Yuöö “glɛɛn ya =nëng mɛ bhɛa”</h>


  =Ya kë =dhɛ ‘yuöö “glɛɛn “iin pë “wɛɛ ‘bha =ya =nëng mɛ ‘bha bhɛa” kö a bho mü kɔ “slë ‘yaa ‘dhö, kö a mɛ ‘yaa “tɛɛ dhɛ yö sië së ‘ka, ‘wɔn ‘ö dhɛ ‘dhö a bha kö ‘ü a kë a mɛ gɔ yö =nɛ:
  
  Blɛɛsü ‘gü, bhö dɔ a mɛ =taama =dhɛ kɔ ‘ö ü “yan ‘dhö -a -bha ‘sëëdhɛ -ta ya- ‘dhö. Ü gbe nu bɔ a gɔ; ü kɔdhɛ da “kʋʋ.
  
A =plɛ naa ’gü, ü kɔdhɛ bha a =nëng a ‘gu ta a bugɔ gɔ “dhuʋ̈ dhɛ waa “sɩga nu =zinngü. Ü kɔ ‘ya ‘dho bɔ a “sɩga ta.

  A yaaga naa ‘gü,a ‘gu bha a bhloo “gbɩɩ ‘ka ‘ko ta ‘gbɛ ‘ka kö “tɛɛ yö ‘go a gɔ “sia =yën -yö da. “Kɛɛ bhöö bhloo “vaandhö ‘ko ta ‘gbɛ ‘ka. ‘Bha a kë “dhʋ̈ “tɛɛ yö dho ‘go a tong ‘gü ‘ö ‘pë ‘ö bhɛa” bha a bho mü. Ü mɔɔ a bha ‘ü a kë a gɔ “dhʋ̈ pinngpinngdhö “ni kö ‘yaa ‘go sië ‘mü.
  
￹￹=Ya kë ‘zü =dhɛ ‘mɛ ‘ö pë ‘ö =nëng a bhɛa” bha faan ya kë a bha =ya ziö- ‘ka ü ta, kö “yan së ‘yaa a gɔɔ ‘zü, a ‘waannu =dhɛ kɔ ‘ö ya a ‘dhö “vaandhö:

A wɔ ö ko ta. Bhö dɔ a ta =dhɛ kɔ ‘ö ya a ‘dhö. Ü kɔ =plɛ bha a wɔ ‘ko –ta, a bugɔ waa “sɩga =zinng ‘gü. =Nëng a ‘gu bha ta “gbɩɩ ‘ka “kɛɛ “vaandhö wɔn ‘ka kö “tɩng yö da. A kë “dhʋ̈ ‘ko ta ‘gbɛ ‘ka “ni kö ‘pë bha ‘yaa ‘go sië ‘mü.
﻿
<h>2 “Yua ‘ö mɛ kë mɛ ga yö ‘ko “dhiʋ̈ dhɛ nu ‘gü (=Gla “kpɛa)</h>

“Yua ‘ö mɛ kë mɛ ga yö ‘ko “dhiʋ̈ dhɛ -nu ‘gü bha, ‘mɛ ‘ö ‘yii a kë së, yö mɔɔ a bha ‘ö mɛ “pɛɛn do ga a bha.

‘Mɛ ‘ö ‘bha ga =dhɛ ü ga yö ‘ko “dhiʋ̈ dhɛ nu wo bhɔ wɛɛndhö, ‘ö “yi nu ‘wo kan nu wo “slʋ̈ʋ̈dhö, ‘bha ‘dho ü de sëë bho ‘zü, a “dhɛ “gbɩɩ ‘ö ‘dhö a ga ‘ö ya:

Mlü “flɩɩ bha, yɛɛn” “piʋ̈ kö bhii ‘dho yi ‘gü, ‘yö ‘ü a “sang ‘në yan yiisiö dan. Pë bhö ‘ka “sang =në ‘ö ‘kwa wɩ a ‘ka. ‘Bha a dan ‘yö ‘ü dɔ “yëë ( kö kwa pö ‘ü “yi sɛa=loo bha). “Yi bha yö ‘to bha “dhʋ̈ kö dhɛ yö =kpaɔ. 

‘Bha bö dhia” “piʋ̈ kö ‘bhii pë ‘bha bhö =kö, ‘yö ‘ü “siʋ̈ ya. “Yi ‘dhɛ ‘ö wɔ mlü “flɩɩ bha ‘ö kë “yi blɛɛsü ‘ka bha, ‘yö ‘ü a bho a bha, ‘ü “yi dee “wɛɛ ‘në ‘bha =loo pë ‘në ‘bha ‘‘gü, ‘ü dɔ “siʋ̈ ta ‘ü mlü ga bha, a =loo ‘gü. ‘Bha ga =dhɛ yöö ya “tɛɛ sü bha bhoo, ‘yö ‘ü bho “siʋ̈ ta, ‘yö “yi =plɛ naa bha ‘ü bho a bha ‘zü, ‘yö ‘ü “yi “wɛɛ ‘bha =loo bha, ‘ü dɔ “siʋ̈ ta. Yaa pö yöö ya “tɛɛ sü bha, ‘yö ‘ü a bho ‘mü, ‘ü “yi ‘dhɛ bha, a bho bha. Kö ya kë “yi yaaga naa ‘ka.

‘Yö ‘ü a dee “wɛɛ ‘bha =loo pë do bha ‘gü ‘ü mlü bha a =loo =bhaa. Yaa pö yöö “tɛɛ, ‘yö ‘ü- bho ‘mü, ‘yö “yi bha ‘ü bho bha, ‘ü a dee ‘bha= loo bha, ‘ü dɔ “siʋ̈ ta. Yöö “tɛɛ, ‘yö ‘ü- bho ‘mü, ‘ü “yi ‘dhɛ bha a bho bha.=Ya kë “dhʋ̈ kö “yi ‘ö ‘ü a ziö mlü ga bha, a bha “dhia “piʋ̈ bha, ü a ziö a bha ‘ko ta yiisiö. A ‘dhɛ ‘ö wɔ a bha ‘ö dhɛ yö =kpaɔ bha, ya da mü kö ya kë “sɔɔdhu. =Ya ‘go mü ‘yö ‘ü mlü ‘ö ya dhëë “kan bha ‘ü bhö, ‘ü =gban bhö. ‘Bha ü bo a bhö sü ‘ka, kö ‘bhaa bhii pë “wɛɛ ‘bha bhö a ziaan ‘gü “dhɛdhɛ yiisiö “piʋ̈. 

A “sunma yö kë =dhɛ kö ‘ü a bhö “dhɛdhɛ “saaga (8) -naa ‘ka dhia” “piʋ̈, kö bhii ü “yan ‘to ‘yënng ya mɛ gɔ =zinng ‘gü “tʋ̈ng ‘ö kë=mingdi ‘ka bha,=në a gɔ kö ‘ü gun naa pë bhö.

(Ü dho a kë “dhʋ̈ dhɛkpaɔyi kɔng =plɛ ö ga “saaga “piʋ̈. ‘Waa wlö dhɛkpaɔyi “wɛɛ ‘bha ta tongtongdhö. ‘Bha kë “dhʋ̈ kö ‘bha “kian zë. Kö bhii a zü dee bho.

A mlü ga “yi “nangglüü nangglüü ‘ö yöö da ü ga yö ‘ko “dhiʋ̈ dhɛ nu ‘gü bha, =në yöö dhii nu ‘ö ‘wo mü, ‘ö ‘wo ü ga ‘gü dhɛ nu bhɔ sië bha, a nu bho ‘mü.

Dhɛkpaɔyi kɔng =plɛ ö ga “saaga bha kö ‘ü nu yö ‘ko “dhiʋ̈ kö ‘bha ü de dha dedewo. Ü dho kë “klʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈.

=Bɛdhɛ “gbɩɩ =në ‘ö ‘ü ga naa bhaa ‘gü bha.
﻿
<h>3 Dhebë ‘ö ‘gbiöö ‘ö dho kë kɔ ‘ö bha kö yö ö ‘në ‘kpɔ yi dɔ</h>

Kɔ ‘ö dho, ö ‘në ‘kpɔ “tʋ̈ng dɔ ‘ka yö nɛ:

Dhebë bha, ö kɔ “zu kɔ to =taama sü ‘ö a kë, “iin ‘ö bɔ ‘ka dhebë nu bɔ dhɛ ‘gü bha, ‘ö sü dhɛkpaɔyi to =taama sü bha bha, yö “su yaaga bho “dhiʋ̈, “iin “kan- “dhiʋ̈. =Ya ‘go mü kö yö dhɛkpaɔyi “saɔplɛ (7) zuö a ta.

A “sunman yö kë =dhɛ kö a bha kɔ “zu sü dhɛkpaɔyi to =taama sü yö kë “su ‘ö kë “kwi a “su ‘ka, ‘ö kë zangvie ‘ka bha, a dhɛkpaɔyi kɔngdo (10) ‘ka, kö kwaa dhong =ni: zangvie dhɛkpaɔyi kɔngdo, =wa “su yaaga “kan “dhiʋ̈ kö yö dho bɛ “su ‘dhɛ ‘ö ‘wo dhɛ Ɔkötɔbrë “kwi wo ‘gü bha, a dhɛkpaɔyi kaɔng do –bha. =Ya kë “dhʋ̈, =wa dhɛkpaɔyi “saɔplɛ da a ta, kö ya kë Ɔkötɔbrë dhɛkpaɔyi kɔngdo ö ga “saɔplɛ. Kö “tʋ̈ng ‘ö bha a zü dhɛ bha yö dho ‘në ‘kpɔ ‘ka. Kö dhɛkpaɔyi kɔng do ö ga “saɔdo, ö ga “saɔplɛ, ö ga “saaga waa ö ga “suɩsiö bha, yö dho ‘në ‘kpɔ a do ‘ka.

=Ya kë “dhʋ̈, kö yö së kö ‘mɛ ‘ö a “piʋ̈ ‘ö ö ‘në ‘kpɔ yi dɔ, yö ö “tʋ̈ng kë dhɛkpaɔyi tomaasü ‘ö “su yö a ‘ka bha, a ‘gü.
﻿
<h>4 Köng bhɛ “sɛɛ bha =bɛdhɛ “gɩɩ mü</h>

Dhebë nu ‘ö ‘wo ‘gbiöö ‘ö nu gɛn =ya bhla, a nu bha=bɛdhɛ do =nɛ:

Köng (“Maa “sɛ ‘gü mɛ nu wo woo pë dhɛ kpɛa) bhɛ “sɛɛ ‘ö bha, =bɛdhɛ së dede mü dhebë nu ‘ö ‘wo ‘gbiöö ‘ö nu gɛn =ya bhla, a nu bha ‘ka. ‘Wo dho a kë kɔ ‘ö bha, yö =nɛ: köng bhɛ “sɛɛ ‘ö bha, waa kun =kwɛɛ tiantiandhe bho, “iin ‘zü a ‘dhɛ ‘ö dho =mɔɔ a nu =kwɛɛ tiantiandhe ‘ka, waa ‘sü, ‘yo ‘wo a kpa së ‘ka, a “yi ‘ö bha, ‘yö ‘wo a “vɛdhɛ yan do “iin =plɛ mü.
﻿
<h>5 kwi ‘kun –yua</h>

Kwi ‘kun bha, “yua kpɛnngdhö ‘yaa mü. Yö kë “yua nu =në a nu =keng. Kwi ‘kun bha, yöö dede ‘ö ‘ya dhɛ ‘ö bha, yö mü, a bha da ‘gü da ‘ö wo naa =sië “gbɩɩ ‘ka dedewo ‘në ‘sɛɛnnë nu gɔ bha, a ‘ka.

=Ya kë =dhɛ ‘mɛ ‘ö “yua ‘dhö bha kö “nɛnɛ yö nu ta, ka sɔ bho a mɛ bha “pɛɛpɛdhö. =Ya kë ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka, -ka sɔ ‘ö bha bha, a gban bho a bha “pɛɛpɛdhö =dhɛ kɔ ‘ö ‘në ‘dhö wɔ a ‘ka ö ‘kpee ‘ka ya- ‘dhö.

A kë sü ‘ö =dhɛ kɔ bha ‘dhö, ‘yö së. ‘Ka sɔ bho  a bha ‘yö “nɛnɛ “bhʋ̈ ‘dhö =lɔɔ.

‘Yaa së kö ‘ka a kë =dhɛ kɔ ‘dhɛ ‘ö ya ‘dhö.

=Ya kë “dhʋ̈ “nɛnɛ da ‘gü =në ‘ö da “yuamɛ bha gɔ.

=Ya ‘go mü ‘mɛ “ʋʋ ‘mɛ ‘ö “nɛnɛ ‘ö a mɛ bha, yö së kö a mɛ yö “yi mü, yö “dhü bhɛ nu “yi mü.

=Ya kë ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka, yö “yi ‘ö =ya “tɛɛ ‘ö =ya =dhiëë bha, a mü. 

Dhɛa” ‘kpɔ: 

Yö “dhʋ̈ tɛan ‘ka =dhɛ ‘në nu ‘wa ‘dho “sukadhu pë nu bhö, =ya kë “dhʋ̈ kö bhië” ‘në nu woo gɔɔn a nu ‘gü ee ?

A yɔɔ: =sua mü. “Sukadhu pë nu bha ‘waa bhië” ‘në da ‘në nu ‘gü. “Sukadhu pë nu bhö sü bha, yö dho a nu gba “sɔn kë =në a ‘ka. A gɛn mü =dhɛ ‘në nu ‘ö ‘wo bha, a nu =miëë ‘gü dhɛ ‘ö a nu “sɔn ‘dhö gban sü ‘ka ‘gü bha, ‘yii kian =kö. A kë “dhʋ̈ sü bha ‘gü, ‘pë ‘ö bha “nɛɛ nɛɛ dhɛ ‘ö ziö sü ‘ka naa ‘gü waa pë “wɔ sü kö wa nu bhö, ‘në nu bha a nu “sɔn nu wo dho see.

=Ya ‘go mü, kö ‘në nu wo nëng kë “sukadhu pë nu bhö sü bha ‘gbɛ, bhöpë kpɛnngdhö bhö sü faan ‘yaa kë a nu ‘gü.

Yö “dhʋ̈ tɛan ‘ka =dhɛ ‘yaa së kö ‘në nu wo tɔyaan bhö, =ya kë “dhʋ̈ kö woo kë =kwan mɛ nu ‘ka ee?

A yɔɔ: ‘Aa bhoo, =sua mü. A dhɛ ya bha ziaanwo kö wa bhö. A gɛn mü =dhɛ tɔyaan bha yö mɛ kwi ‘gü dhɛ bha pë së dede =në ‘ka. A wɔn ‘gü ‘në nu bhawɔn ya bha kö wa bhö.

Yö “dhʋ̈ tɛan ‘ka =dhɛ “dhü bhɛ nu ‘ö ‘wo kë nu wo =dhɛ dhöng (seɩ”) nu, =goyaa nu ‘dhö bha ‘mɛ ‘ö ‘kpin “iin kwi ‘kun ‘dhö bha, a mɛ ‘ya ‘dho a bhö ee?

A yɔɔ: =sua mü. A dhɛ dede ziaan ya bha kö a mɛ yö “dhü bhɛ nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈, ‘ö da ‘ka ziaanwo a “wɛɛ ‘bha nu bha bha, kö a mɛ ya bhö kö ya nu “yi nu mü.
﻿
<h>6 ‘Yuöö “glɛɛn =ya =nëng ü bhɛa” (2)</h>

‘Ü pë bhö sië kö ‘yuöö “glɛɛn yö =nëng ü bhɛa”, ‘yuöö ‘ö go ‘tɛɛ dede ‘ö gü bha, ü =wee pa ‘ka kɔngga “iin ‘zü ‘tɛa ‘gü pa ‘ka kɔngga bha, a ma ‘tɛɛ dede bha a “tʋ “dhiʋ̈ pinngpinngdhö. Yö dho ‘to ‘ka “dhʋ̈ ‘ö ‘yuöö “glɛɛn bha ‘ö =lɔɔ, ‘ö go ü bhɛa”, ‘ö kë ü dhasü ‘ka.
﻿
<h>7 Bhangglöö(bandhe), =bɛdhɛ “gbɩɩ mü</h>

Bhangglöö bhɛ ‘ö ya pëkë (tan) bha, yö mɛ gba pëbhee ‘wɛɛ ‘bha nu bhö dhɔ ‘ka.

‘Mɛ nu ‘ö faan ‘yaa a nu bha, “iin ‘ö =wa kë zii , ‘ö wü waa tɔyaan nu bhö sü =ya kë a nu bha “gbɩɩ bha, a dhɛ ya bha kö wo bhangglöö pëkë sü bhö “tʋ̈ng ‘gbɛ dhɛ ‘gü.

‘Mɛ nu ‘ö wü waa tɔyaan nu bha a nu bhö sü ‘ö nu bha “gbɩɩ, waa pö woo a nu bhö, wo mɔɔ a bha ‘ö ‘wo nu bhö bhangglöö pëkë sü ‘ka.

‘Mɛ ‘ö bhië” ‘në =ya gɔɔn a ‘gü, a =bɛdhɛ =nɛ. A mɛ yö bhangglöö pëkë sü ‘sü, (“Maa mɛ nu wa dhɛ bandhe). A ga ‘ö ‘gü bha ya bho ‘gü, ya “zu, ya ‘kpɔ ‘yënng dhɛ. =Ya ga, ‘yö a bi bho. A bi bha yö mɔɔ a bha ‘ö pa, “iin ‘ö a =kaan “bhaa “puu ‘ka, “iin mɔni ‘ka ‘ö bhö. 

Bhië” ‘në =bɛdhɛ “gbɩɩ bha. A mɛ ya ‘gü dan.
﻿
<h>8 ‘Ü “ta ‘sü sië kö kpaa ‘në yö ‘dho ü “yënng</h>

A ‘bha nu =ya kë, ‘ü “ta ‘sü sië, kpaa ‘në ‘bha bha yö nu ‘ö sɔ ü “yënng. Yö bhɔ =dhɛ slëë yö bhɔ.

‘Bha ga =dhɛ =ya sɔ ü “yënng, ‘bha ‘dho ü kɔ ziö ü “yan “dhiʋ̈. Ü slëë ‘gü “vaandhö kö ‘ü ü ta ya ziaan ‘ü ‘dho sië ‘ka bha, a gɔ ‘kii ü “yan “pʋ. ‘Bha a kë “dhʋ, yö dho ‘to mü ‘ö go ü “yënng.
﻿
<h>9 ‘Pë ‘ü bhö ‘ö ü “gblü ziö sië, a “gblü ziö ‘ö bha, a =bɛdhɛ =nɛ</h>

  ‘Bha ‘dho ü de sëë bho “wɛɛwɛ =bɛdhɛ “wɛɛ ‘bha mɔɔ sü ‘ka =dhɔtrɔɔ =plöö.
  
  Dhɛ ga, ü “gblü ‘ö ziö sië, bhö =wee bi ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘sü ü kɔngga “iin “sang ‘në “zɔ “dhiʋ̈, ‘ü da pë ‘në ‘bha ‘gü, ‘ü “yi =loo ta. ‘Bha pë ziö ‘gü =ya kaan “kwëë së ‘ka, ‘yö ‘ü mü. ‘Bha ü bo a mü sü ‘ka, ü “gblü blɛɛsü ‘ö dho ziö a ziaan ta bha, =ya ‘go a ‘gü, kö ü bha “gblü ziö bha =ya yën. “Kö ‘zü ‘ö ‘wo pö bhii “ta =gblɛɛn ‘kpɔ =dhɛ mɛ yö go “Maadhö mɛ yö dho ‘Biya, ü “gblü “wɛɛ ‘bha ‘yii ‘dho ziö ziaan ‘ka ‘ü dho ‘ü =loo ‘ka.
﻿
<h>10 ‘Ö ü “piʋ̈ ‘ü kë ü faan ‘gü kpɛɛwo: “nimlɔɔ blɛɛsü</h>

  ‘Mɛ ‘ö “piʋ̈ ‘ö kë ö faan ‘gü “tʋ̈ng =gban ‘gü,‘ö “piʋ̈ “gʋng ‘ya ‘dho ö kë =plɛplɛ, dhia” “piʋ̈ =gban “pɛpɛ ‘gü, a mɛ ya bö kö ‘yii pë “wɛɛ ‘bha bhö =kö, “yi dede ‘ö ya, a sandhe, “iin ‘zü a zuɛɛbhɛ, “kwi yö ö bha pë dhɛ ‘dhiitrë, a mɛ ya do mü. Ya ö bo a kë “dhʋ̈ sü ‘ka, ‘yö yöö pë bhö, ‘yö gun a bhö naa =tɔn. “Kɛɛ a mɛ yö ö ‘gü dɔ “gbɩɩ ‘ya ‘dho pö ‘ö dhɛkpaɔyi nu da a “yi bha a mü sü =zinng ‘gü. A kë “dhʋ̈ sü bha ‘yaa së.
  
  ‘Wɔn ‘ö bha, ‘mɛ ‘ö ya =bhlëë ‘gü dedewo, kö a mɛ =ya ‘wɔn së kë ö de dhɛ.
﻿
<h>11 ‘Ö ü “piʋ̈ ‘ü kë ü faan ‘gü kpɛɛwo: “nimlɔɔ =plɛɛ naa</h>

  Kɔ do ‘ö kë faan ‘gü sü “nimlɔɔ blɛɛsü bha ‘dhö ‘ka, ‘ö gban “yi ‘dhiitrë do mü sü bha bha, ‘yö a ‘dhɛ ‘ö ya, a bha ‘dhö ‘ka. ‘Bha bö dhia” “piʋ̈ kö ‘bhii pë ‘bha bhö =kö, bhö mɛtii dhöng (seɩ”) bhɛ do bhloo kö ‘ü a “yi =loo “vɛdhɛ do ‘gü, ‘ü “yi =loo ta yö “vɛdhɛ bha pa. A kaan “kwëë së dede ‘ka. A mü. “Kɛɛ a kë “dhʋ̈ yi =gban “pɛpɛ ‘ka. ‘Bha kë “dhʋ̈, ü dho kë ü faan ‘gü “tʋ̈ng =gban ‘gü, “gʋng ‘yii ‘dho ü kë =plɛplɛ.
﻿
<h>12 =Mlɛɛ =ya ö “dhidhi -pɛn ü “yënng</h>

  =Mlɛɛ =ya ö “dhidhi =wɛng ü bha mɛ ‘bha “yënng dhɛ ‘ö “dhɔɔkɔ ‘dhö bha a ‘gü, ü ‘gü dɔ “gbɩɩ kö ‘ü “nɔnɔ, ‘ö kë “kwi a “nɔnɔ ‘ka, ‘ö ‘yaa “nɛɛnɛɛ, ‘ö ‘wo dhɛ “kwi wo ‘gü bɔngdhe ‘wluziö bha, ‘ü a do ‘dhɔ kö ‘ü “yi yö ‘mɛ ‘ö =mlɛɛ ‘dhö ö “dhidhi =pɛn a “yënng bha, a “yan ga =plɛ bha a nu ‘gü. ‘Bha kë “dhʋ̈, yö dho kë “klʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈. ‘Wɔn ‘bha bha ‘bha, ‘yii ‘dho a kë tongtongdhö. =Bɛdhɛ “gbɩɩ dede =në ‘ü a -ga sië bha.
﻿
<h>13 “Sɔn kë =bɛdhɛ</h>

  ‘Mɛ ‘ö ü “sɔn ‘dhö ü kë sië, =ya kë =dhɛ ü “sɔng ga ‘ö ü kë sië bha a yɛ ga ‘dhö ‘gü, ‘bha ‘dho ü de sëë bho, =bɛdhɛ ‘ö ya a kë.
  
  Ü “sɔnga bha ‘ö ü kë sië “tʋ̈ng dede ‘ö ‘ka bha, ‘bha ‘dho ‘kɔ =taama kë dhɛ ‘gü, yee” “viëë ‘në ‘bha yö kë ü gɔ. ‘Bha ‘kɔ =taama bha kë, ü ‘gü dɔ “gbɩɩ kö ‘ü ü dega gbo ‘ö bha, ‘ü sɛɛnnë ‘bha ‘sü “dhü ‘në “zɔ “dhiʋ̈ kö ‘ü a ya ‘gü, ‘ü yee” “viëë bha a ya ta. Ü mɔɔ a bha ‘ö ‘ü kë “dhʋ̈ ‘ko ta =plɛ “iin yaaga dhɛkpaɔyi do bha ‘ka. Kö ü gbo ‘ü ya a ‘gü bha, a =fii ‘kö bha yö da ü =miëë bha a “piʋ̈, kö ü “sɔn bha yö dɔ dinngdhö, kö ya kë a bo sü =në a ‘ka bha. ‘yii ‘dho ü kë ‘zü tongtongdhö ‘ö to ‘ka “dhʋ̈ kwɛ ‘gbɛ dede “piʋ̈.
  
  A ‘gü ma ‘ka =dhɛ ü dega gbo mü. A kë ‘“dhʋ̈ sü ‘gü, a yënng ‘ya ‘dho ü kë. Mɛ ‘yaa yënng kë mɛ dha pë gɔ.
﻿
<h>14 Dhiëë =bɛdhɛ</h>

  ‘Mɛ ‘ö dhiëë =ya dɔ ü bha dee ‘gü, bhö bhangglöö (bandhe) bhɛ ‘ö ‘yii pë kë (tan), ‘ö kpo ‘ka bha, a “kplü “kan kö ‘ü a ya ü bha dhiëë bha a ta. Yö dho dɔ “vaandhö. =Ya bo dɔ sü zë a ‘ka, kö a zua wɔn =në ‘ö =ya ‘to.
﻿
<h>15 Bhangglöö dhü “yi</h>

Bhangglöö (bandhe) dhü “yi bha bhië” ‘në =bɛdhɛ “gbɩɩ mü.

A dhü “yi bha, “kaflɩɩ mü ‘ka “sang ‘në “iin ‘zü “sang ‘në ‘sɛɛnnë bha, a do ‘sü kö ‘ü bhangglöö dhü bha, a “yi yan yaaga “iin yiisiö ‘kun a ‘gü. =Ya ‘go mü kö “sang ‘në do bha ‘ü ‘sü kö ‘ü “zɔ “yɔn yan yaaga “iin yiisiö dan a ‘gü =dhɛ kɔ ‘ü bhangglöö bha kë a ‘ka bha ‘dhö. ‘Bha ü bo kö ‘ü a bhangglöö “yi ‘ü dan bha ‘dhö , “zɔ “yɔn ‘ü dan bha ‘dhö, a nu gban =loo “kaflɩɩ “yi “wɔsü dede “vɛdhɛ yan do ‘gü, ‘ü pë ziö a ‘gü kö yö kaan “kwëë së ‘ka, kö ‘ü a mü.

Yö ziö bhië” gɔ =dhɛ mɛ yö më kë.
﻿
<h>16 “Üü dɔn ‘ö ‘në nu kë bha, a =bhɛdhɛ =nɛ:</h>

‘Mɛ ‘ö “üü ‘dhö ü bha ‘në kë sië, a mɛ yö ö “tʋ ‘to së ‘ka kö ya kë =ni:

Yabha suu ‘dhɛ ‘ö ‘wo dhɛ ai “iin lai (a” i, la” yi) bha a mɛ ya “pɛn do “iin “pɛn =plɛ ‘sü. Ya wüü wüü “iin ya =dhiëë. A böö bha, ya ‘sü kö ya =loo “yi “vɛdhɛ yan do ‘ö ya “tɛɛ tiaandhe ‘ka, a =bhaa. A mɛ yö ö kwaa zü “tʋ̈ng kpö ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka. “Kwi nu wo woo pë pö minitö kɔng do. =Ya =dhiëë kö “sang ‘në sɛɛnnë bha, a mɛ ya yan =plɛ “iin yaaga =loo bhöpë “iin müpë “nɛɛnɛɛ ‘bha ‘gü, kö ya kaan ‘ka, ya nu ‘në ‘ö “üü ‘dhö a kë sië bha a dhɛ. “Kɛɛ yö kë ‘në ‘ö a kwɛ ‘yii yö =kö do -bha a ‘ka.
﻿
<h>17 ‘Mɛ ‘ö ‘gu =ya ma bha</h>

‘Mɛ ‘ö ‘gu =ya ‘ma bha (‘ö ‘yaa ö gboo sië) ‘ö dho a kë kɔ ‘ö bha yö =nɛ.

A mɛ yö yabha kpö do ‘sü ya kaan kaan. =Ya ö bo ko ya =loo “yi “vɛdhɛ yan do “iin =plɛ ‘ö =ya “sukadhu da a bha a =bhaa, ya dɔ “siʋ̈ʋ̈ kö yö “tɛɛ “tʋ̈ng kpö ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka (minitë kɔng do “iin kɔngdo ö ga “sɔɔdhu “piʋ̈). =Ya bo “tɛɛ sü ‘ka, =ya =dhiëë, dhia” “piʋ̈, ‘mɛ bha kö ‘yii pë ‘bha bhö =kö, kö ya “vɛdhɛ yan do mü. Yɛɛn” “piʋ̈ kö yöö ‘dho yi ‘gü, kö ya do mü. 

Kö ya kë “dhʋ̈ sü =bhlëë ya, a ‘gu ta yö dho lɔɔ 

“Iin ‘zü ‘mɛ ‘ö a ‘gu =ya ‘ma bha, a mɛ yö mɛtii seɩ” bhɛ do “iin =plɛ ‘sü ya “yi bho ya =loo “yi ‘ö ‘yaa “wɔwɔsü “iin ‘ö ‘yaa sɛa bha ( ‘kwa pö “dhʋ̈ kö kwa a pö “yi ‘kpɔng kpɔng), a =bhaa. Ya kaan ‘ka së ‘ka. =Ya ö bo kö ya mü. “Kɛɛ ‘ö mü sië kö yö “ta ‘sü sië- ‘ka “lɛɛdhö, kë “dhʋ̈ kö yö da a kwi ‘gü së ‘ka, ya ‘gu lɔɔ.




﻿
<h>18 ‘Mɛ ‘ö =gwan =ya “kan ta</h>

‘Mɛ ‘ö =gwan =ya “kan ta ‘ö dho a kë kɔ ‘ö bha kö yö “kan yö =nɛ.

Blɛɛsü ‘gü, a mɛ yö ya “zɛnngdhö.

A plɛ naa,a mɛ yö ö yun bhloo minitë “sɔɔdhu ‘piʋ̈, “iin yö ‘to ‘ka “dhʋ̈ a =gwan yö ‘gbaannu. =Ya kë ‘zü =dhɛ ‘yaa yan sië, a mɛ yö yeɩ” “viëë kpö ‘në nu kë kö ya nu sɔ ö yun “dhi nu bha a nu ‘gü, kö ya nu “zɔ nu ‘to “yɛɛ. =Ya ö bo a kë “dhʋ̈ sü ‘ka kö yö ö yun nu bhloo ‘zü ‘bha wo minitë “sɔɔdhu ‘ka. =Ya ‘go mü kö ya yeɩ” “viëë nu bha a nu ‘to mü “dhɛdhɛ kpö ‘në ‘bha ‘ka, kö yö gun naa a bho ‘mü “lɛɛdhö ö ‘suaan ‘ka.

(‘Mɛ ‘ö =ya kë =sië =sië ‘ö =gwan ‘dhö kan a ta, yö nëng kë nu wo seɩ” ‘ö kë “kwi a seɩ” ‘ka, ‘ö ‘wo a dhɛ orangziö bha ‘dhö, =tanmatii nu ‘dhö, a nu bhö sü bha, kö yö mɛtii seɩ” nu “yi mü.

‘Ö kë sië “dhʋ̈, =gwan ‘yii ‘dho nu ta.
﻿
<h>19 Dɔn “kpɛa =bɛdhɛ: “nimlɔɔ do</h>

‘Mɛ ‘ö dɔn “kpɛa ‘dhö bha, a mɛ yö “kaflɩɩ mü ‘ka “sang ‘në ‘sü, yö “zɔ “yɔn yan do dan a ‘gü ya =loo pë ‘bha ‘gü. Yö “sang do bha ‘sü yö mɛtii seɩ” “yi “sang ‘në yan do ‘dhö, “kwi a we “gbɩɩ, “sang ‘në yan do ‘dhö yö pë yaaga bha, a nu =gban kaan “kwëë së ‘ka. A mɛ =ya ö bo, “sang ‘në bha ‘yö a yan do mü. “dhɛdhɛ yaaga =ya ziö, ‘yö do ‘bha mü.

“Dhɛdhɛ yaaga =ya ziö, ‘yö a do ‘bha mü. A yaaga ‘bha =ya ziö ‘zü, ‘yö a do “wɛɛ ‘bha mü.

“Kɛɛ =ya kë =dhɛ ‘në ‘ö ‘yɔn bha “iin ‘mɛ ‘ö “yua ‘bha, ‘dhö a bha, ‘ö “yua bha ‘ö dɔn ‘dhö “piʋ̈, kö ‘ka ‘dho we “gbɩɩ ‘kö bha, a da “piʋ, ‘ö a mɛ ya mü. A “bin

=Bɛdhɛ ‘ö ‘ka ga naa bhaasü ‘ka bha, =bɛdhɛ “gbɩɩ mü.




﻿
<h>20 Dɔn “kpɛa =tɔɔ =bɛdhɛ</h>

‘Mɛ ‘ö dɔn “kpɛa ‘dhö bha, a mɛ =ya “yi dɔ “siʋ̈ʋ̈, =ya “tɛɛ dedewo së ‘ka, ‘yö a mɛ ‘dhö a =loo “gbʋnggbʋ ‘gü ‘ö ö gɔ dun a ta kö a mɛ =ya sɔ ‘ma ö gɔ waa “gbʋnggbʋ =gban bha. Yaa kë “dhʋ̈ ‘yö a “dhuu bha ‘ö a gan ö “dhi waa ö yun ‘gü. ‘Yö a kë “dhʋ̈, ‘ko ta ‘gbɛ ‘ka dhɛkpaɔyi bha.

‘Mɛ ‘ö a yun ‘gü =ya ta, a mɛ =ya kë =dhɛ kɔ do ‘ö ‘go sië a ma ‘ka, dɔn “kpɛa bha ‘ka bha ‘dhö.
﻿
<h>21 “Kwi naa ‘gbɛsɛɛ ‘yaa ‘mɛ ‘ö gɔ</h>

Dhɛ ‘ö “kwi naa ‘gbɛsɛɛ ‘ö kë “sɔn zu ‘ka pë ‘ka ‘yaa bha, ‘ü dho a kë kɔ ‘ö bha yö =nɛ. “Dhü ‘ö ‘wo =mɔɔ bha ‘ö ‘wo kë ‘gbɛsɛɛ ‘ka, a sɛɛnnë do “kan kö a zü bha ‘ü “zɔ dɔ kö yö kë ziö “sɔn ‘gü pë ‘ka. A gɔ bha, a “zɔ bhö kö a “sɛɛ yö kë, kö ‘ü a ziö ü “sɔn bha.
﻿
<h>22 Dhɛ ‘ö “kwi naa pë böö ‘ö ‘wo wo “sɔn zu a ‘ka ‘yaa bha</h>

=Ya kë =dhɛ pë böö ‘ö ‘wo ya “sɔn zu ‘ka pë “dhiʋ̈ bha, ‘yaa dhɛ ‘ö bha “iin ‘mɛ ‘ö gɔ, a mɛ yö =wee bi ‘në sɛɛnnë waa ‘seng -bi sɛɛnnë kaan “kwëë ya ya “sɔn zu ‘ka pë ta. “Kɛɛ yö “sɔn zu ‘ka pë bha, a dhɛ ‘ö yöö ziö ö “sɔn bha bha, a =tɔɔ =kö blɛɛsü “yi ‘ka kö pë bi bha, yö ‘ma ‘gü së ‘ka. =Ya ‘go mü kö ya ziö ö “sɔn bha. Yö dho a “sɔn ‘zu së ‘ka dedewo.

‘Mɛ ‘ö ‘seng‘yaa a gɔ, yö mɔɔ a bha ‘ö kë =wee bi doseng ‘ka.
﻿
<h>23 ‘Mɛ ‘ö bhɛa” dhɛ =ya ‘to nɛɛsi</h>

  A mɛ yö “yi ‘në ‘bha dɔ pɛng “dhiʋ̈. =Ya ‘kun kö a mɛ ya bho ‘mü yö =wee ‘në ‘bha da a “piʋ̈ ya mü.
﻿
<h>24 ‘Mɛ ‘ö ‘kpin ‘dhö kë sië</h>

=Ya kë mɛ ‘kpii “iin ‘në ‘kpii ‘ka, a mɛ yö “yi ‘ö =wee ‘në ‘bha ‘dhö a bha, a =loo ö =kwɛɛ kö ya “gan ö yun ‘gü.
﻿
<h>25 ‘Mɛ ‘ö yi ‘yaa da sië a “yan –bha</h>

‘Mɛ ‘ö “dhʋ̈ bha, yɛɛn” “piʋ̈, a mɛ yö ö ‘zu “yi ‘wɔɔ wɔɔ ‘ka. ‘Kwa pö “dhʋ̈ kö kwa pö “yi ‘ö ‘yaa “wɔsü “iin ‘ö ‘yaa sɛa. =Ya ‘go mü, a mɛ yö “nɔnɔ “wɔwɔsü “vɛdhɛ yan do mü kö yö gun‘waannu naa. =Ya ‘go ‘bha wo ‘mü, ‘ö sü ‘yënng ya mɛ gɔ =zinng ‘gü “tʋ̈ng bha ‘ö dho ‘ö yö a ‘ka yɛɛn” “piʋ̈ bha, a mɛ ‘ya ‘dho “kaflɩɩ “iin ‘pë ‘ö ‘wo ‘te kë bha, a ‘bha mü tongtongdhö.
﻿
<h>26 Dhioo nu ‘ö ‘ö ‘wo –së kwa –bha ‘ka</h>

Blɛɛsü ‘gü:

‘wëëga ‘në ‘bha =ya kë ‘mɛ ‘ö a gɔ, ‘ö mɛ “piʋ̈ =dhɛ ‘ö ö bha ‘në ta ‘kun kö yö kë ö faan ‘gü së ‘ka “tʋ̈ng =gban ‘gü, a mɛ ‘ya ‘dho we “nɛɛnɛɛ ‘dhɔ ö bha ‘në bha dhɛ. 

A=plɛ naa: 

a mɛ yö tɔyaan nu, “gwɛɛ nu, “nɔnɔ sɛa “iin =kplü ‘kun sü, “iin “dhü bhɛ nu ‘ö ‘wo kë nu wo dhöng (seɩ”), =tanmatii nu, ze nu, “kpako nu, bhangglöö (bandhe) nu, =vokaa nu, “manggloo nu, glɔɔ “nɛɛnɛɛ nu ‘ö da a ‘ka a “wɛɛ ‘bha nu bha bha, a mɛ ya ‘dhɔ ö bha ‘në dhɛ “tʋ̈ng ‘gbɛ dhɛ ‘gü.

A yaaga naa: 

dhebë ‘ö ‘në dee ‘ö gɔ “yɔn bha, ‘pë nu ‘ö ‘kwa go a nu ‘tɔ ma bha, a dhebë ‘ö “dhʋ̈ bha, ya nu bhö “tʋ̈ng ‘gbɛ dhɛ ‘gü, kë “dhʋ̈ kö yö da a ‘yɔn ‘gü së ‘ka, kö yö kaan a “yɔn “yi ‘ka, kö ‘në yaa mü,yö kë ö faan ‘gü së dede ‘ka.

A yiisiö naa: 

baa ‘ö kë bhö baa ‘ka bha, a “dhɛ bha, kwa nëng kë a bhö sü bha. Bhöpë së dede mü. Yö mɛ da mɛ faan ‘gü. Kwa mɔɔ a bha ‘ö ‘kwa a =flügüdhe kë ‘pö.=Ya ‘go mü, “wɩsɩ “dhɛ nu, ze “dhɛ nu, kplɔɔ” “dhɛ nu waa “kwi a ze “dhɛ nu ‘wo bha, kwa mɔɔ a nu bha ‘ö ‘kwa a nu “kpɛa kpɔ ‘ö ‘kwa nu bi bho ‘dodo ‘ka, ‘ö ‘kwa nu =kaan –dee ‘në nu bha “bhaa “yi ‘ka. Yö ‘në nu da faan ‘gü.
﻿
<h>27 “Sɛɛ slëë</h>

A dhɛ ya bha kö ‘kwa “sɛɛ slëë da =sië =sië kwaa bhöpë nu ‘gü, ‘kwa nu bhö ‘ka,. A kë ‘ö ‘kwa dho wo “dhʋ̈ bha, a gɛn mü =dhɛ =ya kë “dhʋ,̈ yö dho kwa gba pë bhö dhɔ nu ‘ka, ‘ö ‘nii da kwa ‘gü.

‘Mɛ ‘ö a “piʋ̈ ‘zü ‘ö kë “tan bho mɛ ‘ka, a mɛ yö mɔɔ a bha ‘ö “sɛɛ slëë bha a bhö “zɔ “yɔn ‘ka “iin “sukadhu ‘ka. ‘Mɛ ‘ö yaa kë “dhʋ̈ ‘ko ta ‘gbɛ =sië =sië, a mɛ wo yö dho dhi =dhɛ maa ‘në ‘bha ‘ö “tan bho naa dhɛkpaɔ “dhiʋ̈ ‘ö a wo ‘dhö së bha, a ‘dhö.
﻿
<h>28 Bhöpë ‘bha ‘ö ‘wo dhɛ “kwi wo ‘gü karɔtö, a kë yë</h>

Blɛɛsü ‘gü,

karɔtë bha, dhebë ‘ö ‘gbiöö kö ya =dhiëë, ya “yi bho, kö “tʋ̈ng ‘ö ‘ka ‘gbiöö bha yö nëng kë a “yi mü sü bha, a ‘në ‘kpɔ sü ‘yaa =gbɔɔn, ‘yaa kë “gbɩɩ.

A =plɛ naa,

‘në ‘ö a “gblü ‘dhö ziö sië yaa “yi mü, a bha “gblü ziö yö yën.

A yaaga naa,

‘mɛ ‘ö a ga yö ‘ko “dhiʋ̈ dhɛ nu =wa ‘to nɛɛsü, =ya nëng kë a “yi mü sü b̄ha, yö kë “klʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈.

A yiisiö naa,

‘mɛ ‘ö nëng kë a “yi mü sü bha, ‘yaa kë zii “vaandhö. A gɛn mü =dhɛ pë ‘bha -nu -wo kwa =yɔɔn ‘gü, ‘ö ‘wo “slë =mɔɔ- -bha kö -wo kwa kë zii; kɔrɔtë “yi bha -yö -ziö -a nu gɔ zë -sü -gɔ.
﻿
<h>29 Më ‘ö ‘kwa dho a bhö kö kë “klʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈sü yö kë kwa gɔ.</h> “Yua nu ‘ö bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘waa tiaandhe ‘wo nu mɛ dhɛ

‘Mɛ ‘ö “dhʋ̈ dodo ‘ka, a bhawɔn ya bha kö yö pëbhee së bhö, kö yö ba tiaandhe ‘ka, yö kë ö faan ‘gü, yö yë kë dedewo ö kë kɔ ta “klʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ dhɛ ‘gü kpɛawo.

“Yua ‘gbɛ dhɛ wo mü =dɛɛ ‘ö a nu gɛn ‘dhö gban bhöpë nu bha =mɔɔ ‘ö ‘yaa bho mɛ ta ‘kɔdhi ‘gü bha, a nu bha.

‘Mɛ nu ‘ö faan ‘yaa a nu bha “iin ‘ö ’waa wo de =slɔɔ dhɛ yö “yua gɔ bha, a gɛn mü =dhɛ ‘waa pëbhee tiaandhe ‘ö a dhɛ ‘dhö bha wa bhö, a nu bhö; “iin pëbhee ‘yaa =mɔɔ a nu ta. ‘Mɛ nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha, bhöpë saan ya nu bha. A wɔn ‘gü “yua nu ‘ö ‘wo ‘mɛ nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha a nu “dhiʋ̈ =slɔɔ wo ‘gbɛ. 

=Ya kë ‘në ‘sɛɛnnë nu ‘ka, “yua nu ‘ö nu kë bhöpë saan kë sü “gblʋʋ “piʋ̈, wo =nɛ: 

* =Ya kë “dhʋ̈ ‘waa “gla, ‘waa ba wo ba kɔ ta. ‘Waa faan ‘sü.

* Wo to “sia, “iin gleng tiaandhe ‘yaa kë a nu bha. 

* A nu ‘gu yö dɔ a nu “dhiʋ̈ ‘ö nu dɔɔ nu (gbe nu waa nu gɛn nu) ‘wo kë “kangkang nu ‘ka.

* A ‘në nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha, wo kë “wɔɔn wɔɔ “iin a nu “dhiʋ̈ yö kë “nuaa nuaa ‘ka.

* A nu gɛn nu, a nu wë nu waa nu kɔ nu wo kë nu wo bhlasü ‘ka. A ‘bha nu =ya kë bhiëë “iin pë ‘bha yö wo nu wo a nu kwi bha.

* ‘Në nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha, “gblü ziö yö gwëë a nu bha. Mɛtii =bɛdhɛ waa “kwi =bɛdhɛ nu bha, wa nu gba ‘ka, “kɛɛ ‘yaa yan. A “gblü ziö ‘yaa yën 

* A ‘bha nu =ya kë, “yua ‘bha nu yaan yö kë a nu ‘gü, ‘ö a kë “dhʋ̈ sü bha ‘gü, ‘ö dhiëë nu ‘wo dɔ a nu bha “vaandhö “vaandhö, “iin ‘ö nu “tʋdhɛ nu ‘wo bhla nu wo =sië. A ‘bha nu ‘ka ‘zü, a nu “bhluu nu bha bhiëë yö ya a nu bha.

* ‘Në nu ‘ö bhöpë saan ‘ö kë a nu bha ‘kɔdhi ‘gü “dhʋ̈ bha, a mɛ ‘bha nu gɔ “dhɛ yö kë “waan waan “iin wun ‘gbɛ ‘yaa kë a nu =gwinng.

*A nu “yan ‘gü yö kë “luu luu. 

=Ya ‘go ‘në nu bha nu ‘gü, mɛ “gblʋ̈gblʋ̈ ‘dhɛ nu ‘ö ‘wo to, ‘ö woo =de ‘pö bhöpë saan ‘ö nu bha bha, ‘pë ‘ö nu “dhiʋ̈ =slɔɔ a ‘gbɛ dhɛ ‘gü yö =nɛ:

* Mɛ ‘bha nu bha, faan ‘yaa kë a nu bha. =Ya ‘go mü a nu sëë =në ‘ö bho ‘gbɛ.

* Pë bhö sü faan ‘yaa kë anu gɔ.

* Bhiëë ‘yaa “kan a nu “dhi “gʋ̈ng “piʋ̈ dhɛ nu ‘gü.

* A nu gɛn nu wo kë bhla sü nu ‘ka “iin ‘zü ‘gbinki gbinki ‘ka.

“Yua ‘bha nu wo mü a nu gɛn yö mɔɔ bha ‘ö gban ‘wɔn “wɛɛ ‘bha nu bha, “kɛɛ a gbɛ dhɛ ‘gü, yö sü pebhee yaa bhö sü nu bha.

A “yua nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha, wo mü:

mɛ zuë” ta ma sü nu, mɛ “tʋ ‘gü vi sü nu, =gbaɔdhɛ bha ‘në nu ‘sü sü nu, gɔ ‘gü ‘wü nu, =gwan bha kan mɛ ta sü nu, mɛ kwi bha “kpɛa ‘kpɔ sü nu, “yua bha ya mɛ “bhluu bha sü nu waa mɛ zuë” kë nɛɛsü sü ‘ö ‘wɔn nu ‘gü, a nu ‘ka.

Kwaa ‘wɔn dɔ ‘ka =dhɛ pebhee tiaandhe bhö sü bha, yö mɛ dhü takɔɔ “yua nu gɔ. Bhöpë së nu bha, wa kë ‘ö mɛ kwi ‘ö dɔ “yua gɔ gɔn yan ‘gü.

•  Yö së kö ‘kwa a dɔ ‘ka =dhɛ bhöpë ‘ö ‘yaa tiaandhe, a bhö sü bha, yö mɛ gba “yua ‘gbɛ ‘ö ‘kwa ‘go sië nu ‘tɔ ma- bha, a nu ‘ka. =Ya ‘go mü “yua ‘dhɛ “ʋʋ ‘dhɛ ‘ö nu ‘mɛ ‘ö pebhee saan ‘dhö bha, a mɛ gɔ, a mɛ ‘yaa =mɔɔ bha kö yö dɔ a “yua bha gɔ gɔn yan ‘gü. A gɛn mü =dhɛ kö faan ‘yaa a mɛ bha.
• 


• ‘Në nu ‘ö ‘waa pë tiaandhe bhö bha, kö “glüziö yö nu a gɔ, yö kë “gbɩɩ. A ‘gbɛ dhɛ =ya kë, a nu gɔ yö to a ‘gü.
• 
• =Kpiëë kaa ‘gü, ‘yaa së ‘në nu ‘ö pëbhee saan ‘ö nu bha ‘kɔdhi ‘gü, a nu bha ‘ka. A gɛn mü =dhɛ yö mɔɔ a bha ‘ö nu zë.
• 
• ‘Në nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha, foodɔn ‘yaa “kan a nu kpö ‘gü. =Ya ‘go mü yaa pö yöö a nu kë, ya nu kë dedewo.
• 
‘Mɛ nu ‘ö bhöpë saan ‘ö nu bha bha, “yua “wɛɛwɛ dë ‘ö kë ‘kpin ‘ka ya, yaa nu kë, yö gwëë a nu bha ‘ö kë “gbɩɩ. 

Pëbhee tiaandhe bhö sü bha, yö “yuamɛ ta kun ‘ö kë “klʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ “vaandhö.

Pëbhee tiaandhe yö “yua bhɔ mɛ ‘kataa =gblɛɛn, ‘ö go ‘mü ‘ö kë ‘ö “yuamɛ bha ‘ö kë “klʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ “vaandhö. Yö =në a wɔn ‘gü, ‘yö “yua ‘dhö ‘mɛ ‘ö kë sië, a dhɛ ‘dhö a bha kö a mɛ yö pë tiaandhe bhö.

Bhöpë nu ‘ö kwa dhü bhawɔn ‘dhö nu bha kö ‘kwa nu a dhɛ 

Bhöpë nu ‘ö̈ kwa bhawɔn ‘dhö nu bha kö ‘kwa a –nu bhö kö ‘kwa ‘to kwa faan ‘gü së ‘ka “tʋ̈ng =gban ‘gü bha, a nu gɔɔ yö yiisiö. A dhɛ ya bha kö ‘pë ‘ö ‘kwa dho a bhö yi =gban ‘ka bha, ‘kwa a nu ‘sɛɛnnë ‘sɛɛnnë ‘sü a gɔɔ yiisiö bha a nu ‘gü dɔɔndhö ‘kwa a nu da ‘ko “piʋ̈ kwaa pëbhee ‘ö dhɛkpaɔyi bha, a ‘gü.

Bhöpë gɔɔ yiisiö ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha a,

kpö gɔɔ blɛɛsü mü:

1) bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘wo kwa =nëng, kwa tëng, kwa zuë” ga waa kwa dhɛ “wɛɛ ‘bha nu ‘ö ‘wo kwa ‘gü a nu gɔ yö ‘kwëë së ‘ka, wo mü. Bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha wo =në ‘ö mɛ yaa nu bhö ‘yö mɛ yö =kpɛa mɛ kpɛa kɔ ta së dede ‘ka. ‘Mɛ ‘ö “piʋ̈ ‘ö kë ö kwi ‘gü, ‘ö kë ö faan ‘gü a dhɛ ya bha kö dhɛkpaɔyi =gban ‘ka yö bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha, a nu bhö tiaandhe ‘ka ya zo ‘kun. “Kɛɛ yö kë a ‘dhɛ nu ‘ö ‘wo tun së, ‘ö ‘wii see kö a nu ‘ka.

Wo mü: 

1) tɔyaan, wü, tɔ, ‘yuöö “kpɛa, “nɔnɔ, “nɔnɔ =kplü ‘kun sü, =kɛnng, “tʋʋ dhɛ ‘gü -pë nu ‘ka.

2) A ‘dhɛ ‘ö ‘wo dɔ a dhɛ nu bha a nu “piʋ̈ wo mü:

ze “kpɛa, “gwɛɛ, ze suu ‘ö ‘wo dhɛ ‘sozia, , kplɔɔ”, karɔtö, 

3) ‘Yö a ‘dhɛ nu ‘ö nu ga doseng në ‘ö bhöpë ‘ka =dhɛ mlü ‘ö ‘wo a zɔn wöng ‘ka a ‘dhö, “klëën nu ‘dhö, ‘wo dɔ mü. 

Bhöpë “pɛpɛ ‘ö ‘kwa ‘go sië a nu ‘tɔ ma bha, yö së kö ‘kwa a nu kaan “kwëë kwaa pëbhee ‘gü. ‘kwa a nu bhö. Kwa mɔɔ a bha ‘ö ‘kwa:1, 2, 3 nu bha, a nu ‘bha ‘në ‘bha =kaan “kwëë kwaa pëbhee nu ‘gü. Kwaa kë “dhʋ̈ yi =gban ‘ka. 

A kpö gɔɔ =plɛ naa: bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘wo “siʋ̈ ya mɛ kwi ‘gü, ‘ö ‘wo ‘nii da mɛ ‘gü

Bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha, wo =dhɛ “wɔ ‘ö ya “siʋ̈ bha, a ‘dhö. ‘Mɛ ‘ö yë kë “gbɩɩ dedewo, a bhawɔn ya bha kö ya nu bhö. Wo mü pë “nɛɛ nɛɛ nu waa a ‘dhɛ nu ‘ö ‘wo kë =dhɛ baa nu ‘dhö a nu ‘ka. “Kɛɛ ‘yaa së kö mɛ yö mɛ gɔ gban woo doseng zë a nu bhö sü nu ‘gü. Ya kë “dhʋ̈ faan yö go mɛ bha. “Sukadhu pë nu bha wo mü: “sukadhu dede ya a ‘dhö, “zɔyɔn ‘dhö, glɔɔ “nɛɛ nɛɛ ‘dhö, a nu ‘ka. 

=Ya ‘go mü, ‘pë nu ‘ö ‘wo kë =dhee kë pë nu ‘ka woo =de ‘pö kwa bhawɔn ya nu bha.

Wo në ‘ö ‘wo kë =dhee ya pë nu waa bhɛ ya pë nu ‘ka. Wo mü: köng, mlü, “klëën, “wɩsɩ, “kuu, baa, “plëë, =piaa glɔɔ, waa ‘dhɛ nu ‘ö ‘wo bhɔ “wɩsɩ bha ‘ö “kwi ‘dhö dhɛ ‘pɔmö dö ‘tɛɛ, gën, doo, =kɔnng kɔnngblë nu ‘ö da a ‘ka a “wɛɛ ‘bha nu  bha, a nu ‘ka. 

A kpö gɔɔ yaaga naa mü:

“Yɔn pë nu ‘ö ‘wo kë: wü “yɔn nu, “yɔn ‘ö wo da “tʋʋ bha nu, “tukpɛ “yɔn nu, “kwi a ‘pë ‘ö ‘wo da ‘bluu ‘gü ‘ö ‘wo dhɛ ‘bëë, a nu, bhöpë nu ‘ö wo kë “gwɛɛ nu, “dhʋngbhɛɛ nu, ze ‘ö ‘wo dhɛ ‘sozia nu, “kpako nu , =vokaa nu waa “nɔnɔ nu ‘dhö, a nu ‘ka. 

A ‘dhɛ ‘ö ‘kwa ‘go sië a nu ma bha, kwa kwi bhawɔn ya ‘sɛɛnnë ‘sɛɛnnë bha. “Kɛɛ kwaa ‘gü ma së ‘ka =dhɛ, “yɔn pë bhö sü ‘ö ‘wo ziö naa ‘gü bha ‘yaa së.

A kpö gɔɔ yiisiö naa mü

Bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘wo kë kwa dhü takɔɔ pë nu ‘ka “yua gɔ a nu ‘ka. Wo =në ‘ö ‘wo pëbhö sü dhɔ da mɛ bha, ‘ö ‘wo faan da mɛ ‘gü, ‘ö ‘wo mɛ =yɔɔn kë ‘gbɛ .Bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘wo “dhʋ̈ bha wo =në ‘ö ‘wo a kë “dhʋ̈ ‘yö kwa dhü ‘gü dhɛ ‘ö kë tiaandhe, ‘ö kwa =yɔɔn ‘ö “ta sü së dede ‘ka kwa ‘gü. ‘Kwaa nu bhö sië “tʋ̈ng ‘ö a nu ‘gü, “yua yö kwa kë. Woo do bha =në ‘ö ‘wo =yɔɔn da kwa ‘gü. Wo =në ‘ö ‘wo kë “dhʋ̈ ‘yö kwa ga nu, kwa “sɔn nu wo to “slʋ̈ʋ̈slʋ̈ dhɛ ‘gü. 

Wo mü: wü “bhluu nu, tɔyaan nu, ‘yuöö nu, “nɔnɔ sɛa “iin =kplü ‘kun sü nu, ‘pë nu ‘ö ‘wo go “tʋʋ dhɛ ‘gü ( “iin ziaadɛnng ‘gü) nu, “dhü bhɛ nu, “yɔn “puu ‘dhö, a nu ‘ka. Bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘kwa a nu ga bhö =dhɛ mlü ‘dhö, a nu ‘ka.

Mɛ ‘gbɛdhɛ wo pë bhö, “kɛɛ ‘waa a bhö =dhɛ kɔ ‘ö dhɛ ‘dhö bha =dhɛ wa bhö a ‘ka, a ‘dhö. Bhöpë kpökpö gɔɔ yiisiö ‘ö ‘kwa a nu ‘tɔ ma bha, mɛ ‘bha nu zë wo wo gɔ gban a gɔɔ doseng në bhö sü ‘gü. Mlüga ‘dhö, baa ‘dhö, =piaa glɔɔ waa köng (“kpɛa) =në a nu bhö sü ‘gü ‘ö ‘wo dho ‘ka. A kë “dhʋ̈ sü bha ‘yaa së. ‘Ka a kë “dhʋ̈, kö ‘kaa pë bhö tiaandhe ‘ka. bhöpë nu ‘ö ‘wo go a kpö gɔɔ “wɛɛ ‘bha nu ‘gü =dhɛ: tɔyaan ‘dhö, wü ‘dhö, ‘yuöö ‘dhö, ze ‘dhö, “gwɛɛ ‘dhö, “tʋʋ “dhɛ nu, “dhü bhɛ nu waa “wɛɛ ‘bha nu ‘dhö, kwaa nu bhö ‘pö nu wo. A kë “dhʋ̈ sü bha =në pë tiaandhe bhö sü ‘ka. =Ya kë “dhʋ̈ ‘yö mɛ dho ‘to “klʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ dhɛ ‘gü.
﻿
<h>30 “Yan kë yua (Apolo)<h>

Apolo ‘ö ‘mɛ ‘ö kë sië a “dhɛ =nɛ. A mɛ yö baa “dhɛ kpa, a “yi bha, a mɛ ya yö ö “yënng

Yö ziö apolo gɔ =dhɛ mɛ yö më kë.
﻿
<h>31 ‘Mɛ ‘ö bha gɔɔn- -dhɛ ‘yaa –tiaandhe</h>

“Dhü ‘në ‘bha yö dhö, mɛ ‘gbɛ dhɛ wa kë döng “dhü ‘ka. Yö “ziɔɔn ziɔɔn ‘ka =ni. “Gwɛɛtaa mɛ nu wa dhɛ =ziɔnng. A “dhɛ bha, ‘mɛ ‘ö faan ‘yaa a bha gɔɔndhɛ bha, a mɛ ya “dhɛ bho kö ya da “yɔɔ “piʋ̈, yö slëë ‘në ‘bha kë bha, kö ya =gban da ‘kwëë ya nu zɔn. =Ya ö bo zɔn sü ‘ka, ya da we “puu ‘në sɛɛnnë “piʋ̈ ya mü. =Bɛdhɛ së dede mü.
﻿
<h>32 “Yi -bha -go mɛ kwi ‘gü -sü</h>

‘Në ‘gbɛ -dhɛ -wo mü ‘ö “gblü ziö -ya yö -a –nu -bha ‘ö - -nu -gɔ ‘ö to- ‘gü. -A -gɛn -mü =dhɛ “yi =ya ‘go -a -nu kwi ‘gü. “Yi -bha -go mɛ ‘gü -sü bha, -a ‘gbɛ -dhɛ -yö -sü “gblü ziö “gbɩgbɩ -nu në- -a -nu -bha. -Ziaanwo kö -pë -yö -da –a ‘gü, kö -a -ta -kpɛɛ =ya dɔ do. “Yi yö -mɔɔ -a -bha ‘ö go mɛ “gblʋ̈gblʋ̈ -nu kwa kwi ‘gü, “kɛɛ ‘në -nu =në -a -nu -bha ‘dhö “gbɩɩ-. “Yua bha, -ya -nu -zë “vaandhö “vaandhö. =Ya kë “dhʋ̈, kö -yö -së kö ‘mɛ ‘ö “yi ‘ö ‘go sië -a kwi ‘gü, ‘kwa -a -kɔ dɔ. Kwa -dho -a -kɔ dɔ- ‘mü =dhɛ ?

-A -kɔ dɔ -kɔ =nɛ:

* a –mɛ weɩ” ‘yaa kë ‘gbɛ “iin ‘yaa kë -ziaanwo, “iin –yö -kë dhuɛngsü.

* -a –mɛ “kidhʋng –yö -lɔɔ

￹- a “dhi –yö “kpɛɛ -kpɔ

* -a “yan -nu -wo -dho ‘gü, ‘ö -a “yan “yi ‘yaa kë.

* =ya kë -dee ‘në ‘ka, =gwinngdhö -ya -kë.

* -a -mɛ zuë” -ta -yö -ma “vaandhö “vaandhö.

* -a -gɛn waa- -kɔ -nu -wo -kë -sɛa.

* -kwaa -mɛ ‘gu -ta kwi “gan =ni: =Ya kë =dhɛ ‘yaa ‘dho sië ö “gblʋʋ ‘gü “vaandhö -së ‘ka, kö “yi ‘yaa ‘në bha- ‘gü.

‘Mɛ ‘ö “yi ‘ö ‘go sië- ‘gü, -a =bɛdhɛ =nɛ:

-A -mɛ -yö “yi mü ‘gbɛ. -Yö “dhü bhɛ -nu “yi mü. -Yö “tʋʋ “yi “lʋ̈nglʋ̈ng -nu pa. 

‘Pë ‘ö ya -kaa kë kö ‘ka- nu -a -dhɛ: -ka “yi -sanngdhe (-zuɛɛbhɛ) “iin ‘zü ‘dhiitrë do kë “wɔsü. =Ya =dhiëë kö ‘ka “sang “gblʋ̈gblʋ̈ bha, -a-yan =plɛ dan “sukadhu -bi “iin “zɔyɔn, “iin ‘zü “sukadhu kpö “sɔɔdo “iin ‘zü ‘bhawo “sang ‘sɛɛnnë bha, -a -yan “sɔɔdo dan “sukadhu ‘ka. ‘Ka ‘go mü kö ‘ka “sang sɛɛnnë bha, -a -yan do ‘ö- -ta ‘ö “kan -sü ‘ka =wee bi “piëën -piëën ‘ka -a ‘dhö, ‘seng- “yi “Sang ‘në ‘sɛɛnnë -yan do ‘dhö ( “ni kö “yua -mɛ bha ‘yaa -pe sië). Pë “pɛpɛ bha -kaa -nu kaan- “kwëë. =Ya kë ‘në sɛɛnnë “iin -deenë ‘ka, kaa nu- -dhɛ “sang ‘ka. -Kaa nu- -dhɛ -dedewo =sɔbhɛɛ ‘ka. =Ya kë =dhɛ ‘në bha -a “gblü ‘dhö ziö sië, kë “dhʋ̈ ‘ö ‘ka “yi nu -a -dhɛ ‘ö- mü. -Kaa- -bha “yi kë “bhaa “yi “ö ‘wo- kun “bhaa -ta –a ‘ka.

-Kaa nu -a -dhɛ ‘yënng- -kɔ dan “sɔɔdhu “sɔɔdhu ‘ka (minitë “sɔɔdhu “sɔɔdhu ‘ka), -yö ‘to-‘ka “dhʋ̈ -yö -ya ö weɩ” bho –sü -bha -së ‘ka.

=Ya kë mɛ ‘kpii- ‘ka, -yaa pö yöö “yi mü, -yö “yi ‘dhiitrë =plɛ “iin ö -ziö -ta -a mü -dhɛkpaɔyi -bha. 

=Ya kë ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka, ‘yii -a mü ‘gbɛ, -yö kë “yi ‘dhiitrë do -dhɛkpaɔyi -bha.

=Ya kë =tɔn =dhɛ ‘wɔn “pɛpɛ bha ‘ka -nu kë kö ‘yaan -yan sië, -ka ‘dho =dhɔtrɔɔ =plöö.
﻿
<h>33 “Gblü ziö</h>

Ka “gblü ‘dhö ziö sië:

• -ka -bhöpë ‘ö “Kwi ‘dhö- -dhɛ karɔtë bha, -a -kpa “wɛɛwɛ -së ‘ka. =Ya ma, -a “yi ‘dhö oo, -a karɔtë bha ‘dhö oo, -ka =wee ‘në ‘bha kë- -bha kö ‘ka -a “yi bha mü, ‘ka- karɔtë -bhö.
• 
• -Ka gwɛ bhɛ ‘ö go ö -dhü ‘gü -dee ‘gü bha, -a ‘sü. -Kaa “kɛɛ bho- -	bha, kö ‘ka- -da “yi ‘ö “sukadhu ‘dhö- -bha, -a =bhaa. =Ya ‘ma- -bha =së ‘ka, kö ‘ka- mü.
• 
• -Ka glɔɔ -pëkë -sü (tan -sü) -bhö.
﻿
<h>34 “Zɔn “yɔn bha =bɛdhɛ -mü</h>

Miëë -ya kë ü -bha, ‘ö ‘yaa ga sië, “Zɔn “yɔn –ya –a ‘gü.
﻿
<h>1. 'Waa 'wɔn yaa "yɔɔbho 'wɔn yaa 'ka</h>

-Kwɛ -zlaan 'ö ya, -kwɛ -zlaan zii -dede –mü.

"Tϋng 'bha 'gü Gbaa" =plöö, 'yö gɔndë 'në do 'bha bha -a -bha dhebë 'ö 'në gɔɔn- do kpɔ. 'Në 'ö "dhϋ bha, -sëdhɛ 'ö gun- -gɔ -a "suma "yɔɔ 'yaa gun "tϋng 'kö bha- 'gü tongtongdhö.

-A -ga =dhɛkpaɔyi do 'ka, 'yö waa- ö dhe 'wo dho "dhɔɔ 'gü "kwi -pö 'gü Gbiaan =gwinng- . =Dhɛ 'ö dhebë 'në bha 'ö ö bo "dhɔɔ dɔ -sü 'ka, 'yö pö yöö ö yeekë kö 'ö 'dho ö -yɛɛbhaa 'pödhö, 'yö gɔ sü. Gɔ 'ö 'kwa "wɩ sië- 'ka ya kwa -mɔɔ -a -bha 'ö 'kwa- -dhɛ -yakwëë -kë 'gü -gɔ. -A -gɛn -mü =dhɛ -wa -ya 'gü, mɛ =gban -wo wo wë -bɔ 'kwëë-. "Kwi -nu -wo woo- pë -dhɛ basie. -A "tϋng 'ö bha- 'gü, kö ziaan -yö -tun 'ya- -dedewo. Ziaan bha -a -tadhɛ 'bha -yö -gun mü, 'yaa gun -së tongtongdhö. "Yi ga 'kpii- nü 'ö gun -tɔn =plɛ =zinng 'gü. -Wa -tɔn =lɔɔ "wɛ =ni, 'yö 'wo loo pɔng -ta. Pɔng bha- "kan -sü nü 'ö "gbɩɩ- kö -wa 'to =wa -ya -tɔn 'kun -sü -bha. Pɔng 'ö 'kwa "wɩ sië- 'ka ya, 'waa =mɔɔ- -bha kö -wa -zɔn kwaa- pɔng -nu 'ö 'wo =dɛɛ 'pö- -nu 'gü ya, -a -nu -bha -sëdhɛ 'ka. 'Në 'ö bha -a -bha -sëdhɛ -wɔn 'gü, 'dho 'ö 'wo gun- wo sië gɔ 'gü bha, mɛ 'bha -yaa 'sü, -yaa -ga, 'yö mɛ 'bha 'dhö- sü. -A -bha -sëdhɛ -zë -a -zɔn 'ka "wɛɛ 'bha 'yii kë =slɔɔ 'nu do, "iin 'yii 'dho =slɔɔ- "kpʋng =taa 'ö to- 'ka "dhϋ 'ö -kë "dhiëng "dhiϋ 'to -dhɛ -zë -a 'ka. -A -nu -loo pɔng -ta "tϋng -dede bha kö 'në bha -yö 'nëglɔɔn 'në do 'bha -gɔ. =Dhɛ 'ö -kë =dhɛ gɔ -yö -gun zuu" -zuu zuu" kë sië yaa 'ka bha, 'yö 'mɛ 'ö bha 'ö 'në bha- =nëng ö -tong -bha. Kwa- 'wɔn -dɔ =dhɛ gɔ -yaa pö yöö -tɔn 'kun, 'yö -a "dhiϋ "ta 'sü -mɛ -yaa kë, 'yö -ya -ya 'ka -tɔn -bha -bɛng 'ka, kë "dhϋ kö gɔ 'ya 'dho pö 'ö bhɔ ö zü 'ka. =Ya -tɔn 'kun, 'yö gun -naa 'gbaannu.

-A -kë "dhϋ -sü bha- 'gü, -a vuu" -mü -vuu -mü vuu" -mü 'ö gun kë sië bha, kö gɔ -yö =zang "zang kë sië.

"Eke kwa dë -nu -wa -pö : « Piaa" -yaa -mɛ 'yaa- pö kwa ziaan -ta =plɛ. » -kaa -ga, 'yö 'në bha 'ö bɔ 'nëglɔɔn 'në bha- gban -ta, 'yö bɔ gɔ 'ö bha- yɛ 'ka, 'yö -pö "yi =bhaa ; 'yö mɛ =gban 'wo -ya "gbla -sü -bha "gbʋ 'ka =dhɛ : « N dhee" -nu -gblü bhoo, 'ya ga bhoo, -ka "ta yi -dhɛ bhoo. -Zlaan ü =wɛ =ee ? »

Gɔ =sofɛɛ =de 'pö -a -bha 'gü, gɔ =zuu "zuu 'ö kë sië bha nü- -wɔn 'gü 'yö mɛ -nu bha 'wo "wɩ sië bha. 'Yaa- 'wɔn dɔ =dhɛ 'në 'bha -ya -pö "yi =bhaa. 'Kö 'zü yöö- 'wɔn dɔ =zɔɔ =wɛ, -a -dhɛ -ya -bha kö -yö -tɔn 'kun =kö -blɛɛsü kö -yö gun -naa gɔ 'gbaannu ; 'yii kë kë "dhϋ gɔ -yö -dho bhɔ ö zü 'ka, 'ö nu 'ö -pö "yi =bhaa. =Dhɛ 'ö -kë "dhϋ 'yö -tɔn kun 'yö 'dɔɔnnu. =Dhɛ 'ö -kë =dhɛ dhebë 'në bha -yö -gun -a "piϋ =dhɛ 'ö 'dho 'köö -pö ö bha 'në bha- =keng- "yi =bhaa bha, 'yö 'wo- kun kö 'ya dho ö -de zë-. -A -gɛn -mü =dhɛ gun 'ö- wo "dhϋ bha, kö "yi bha =ya pa, kö =ya wɔ "wɛ mɔngdhö -ziisü 'ka =ni. -A 'klɔɔ- -mü =dhɛ -yö -gun "dhϋ dha ban "tϋng 'gü. =Ya 'go mü -a gɔɔn- "piϋ, dhe "piϋ, 'mɛ 'ö yöö kë "yi kë -mɛ -tiaandhe 'ka -a -nu =zinng 'gü mü, 'yaa gun.

"Siasia bha, 'yö 'wo dho =zang -nu -dhɛ Gbiaan =gwinng-. =Dhɛ 'ö 'wo nu 'yö 'wo dhɛa" 'kpɔ -kë -dhɛ -dede 'ö 'në bha 'ö -pö -a -bha bha -a -wɔn 'ka. 'Yö 'wo glɔɔ -dhü do -kan, 'yö 'wo- -zuö -dhɛ -dede 'ö 'në bha 'ö kë -pö -a -bha bha- 'gü, 'yö glɔɔ =gbë bha 'ö dho 'ö -wo -dhɛ 'bha 'gü "yi -gɔ "siaa- =yën mü. 'Wo dho 'dho- wo bhɔɔ" bho mü, kö 'në bha -a =gee nü =wɛɛ, -ya ga. 'Wɔn bha -yö -gun =dhɛ -gblü 'dhö, -yö -gun "gbɩɩ-, -yö -gun -wëësü.

=Dhɛ 'ö -kë "dhϋ 'yö =zang -nu 'wo "klɩɩ -ya dhebë 'në bha- -kɔɔ kö 'ya 'dho ö -de zë-. 'Yö 'wo 'nëglɔɔn 'në bha, -a -bha -kë 'pö "dhϋ, 'yö 'wo dho -a -nu 'ka =zang =plöo Gbiaan =gwinng-, 'yö 'wo dhebë 'në bha- -da 'kɔ do 'bha 'gü, 'yö 'wo 'nëglɔɔn 'në bha, -a -bha -kë 'pö "dhϋ. 'Yö =zang -nu bha 'wo -ziö 'wo dho Gbaa" =plöö. 'Wo =loo mü 'yö dhebë 'në bha -a =gɔn 'ö -dhɛ 'ö -bha 'yö 'wo- -dhɛ -zɔn -a -nu -dhɛ kö waa- ö "tɛɛbë -nu -wo "maa gɔɔn- sië. =Dhɛ 'kö 'wo -kpan -a -bha -zë bho bhoo, "klɩɩ- nü 'ö 'wo- -ya -a -kɔɔ, 'wo nu- 'ka Gbiaan =gwinng-. =Dhɛ 'ö 'wo =loo mü, 'yö 'wo dhebë 'në waa- nëglɔɔn' 'në bha -a -nu yö "kpɛnng. =Dhɛ 'kö dhebë 'në bha 'ö -kpan ö =gɔn -bha, "pɛ 'ö- bho "gbʋ -bha, -a -wo -yö -kë =dhɛ dha "wɩ -wo 'dhö.

=Dhɛ 'ö -kë "dhϋ, 'yö 'wo -ziö 'wɔn bha- 'gü -a =gɔn -dhɛ. 'Yö gɔndë 'në bha 'ö 'dɔɔnnu zuudhö =dhɛ 'mɛ 'ö -kling kling- =ya yö nü wo- -ta 'dhö. 'Yö go 'mü 'ö- pö =zang -nu -dhɛ -wo "klɩɩ bho ö -kɔɔ. 'Yö 'wo- bho mü. 'Yö dho 'ö =yɔɔn nëglɔɔn' 'në bha- "sɔɔ, 'yö ö "yan -gban -a 'gü zuudhö. 'Ö gun kë sië "dhϋ bha, kö =zang -nu -wa =yɔɔn- -nu "sɔɔ mü. 'Yö gɔndë 'në bha 'ö- pö piaa" yaa- -mɛ bha- -dhɛ : « N "tɔngdë, 'wɔn 'ö ü "dhiϋ =slɔɔ bha 'yii kë kë ü =kwɛng- -wɔn 'ka. 'Bhii kë- "dhiϋ wlüü" -a -bha. -Zlaan këwɔn -mü. N 'dhu do -yö 'pödhö, 'ma- nu ü -dhɛ dhe 'ka. Kö -yö kë =dhɛ 'wɔn 'ö -kë bha -ya dhi nü 'ö- wo n -dhɛ, 'yaa -mü, "kɛɛ 'wɔn -yake nü 'ö 'a- -ya... ».

-Dedewo, 'yö gɔndë 'në bha 'ö- pö -kɔ 'ö- -bha, 'ö- -kë -a -kɔta, 'yö 'mɛ bha waa- 'dhu 'wo to wo 'ko -gɔ. 'Në -nu 'ö 'wo- -nu kpɔ, 'mɛ 'ö- -gɔ 'gü 'yii kë kë -së, 'ö 'yii kë 'dho =klang 'ka =gblɛɛn, yö nü 'ö kë -kë =klang- -gɔ -mɛ 'ka, "kɛɛ =klang- -gɔ -mɛ -nu -bha didhɛtëë 'ka. Mɛ "pɛpɛ 'dhɛ 'kö 'wo to, -a -nu =gban -wo kë -kë "kwi -gɔ -mɛ "gblϋgblϋ -nu 'ka.

Gɔndë 'në 'ö bha -ya -zɔn kwa -dhɛ =dhɛ -de -kun 'wɔn "dhiϋ -sü, nü 'ö -së. 'Wɔn -yake -ya -sü, 'ö 'bhaa 'wɔn yaa "yɔɔ bho 'wɔn 'yaa 'ka, nü 'ö -së.
﻿
<h>2. -Dhioo -wo 'yaa ziaan yaa -zɔn mɛ -dhɛ</h>

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do 'ka 'yö laabhölaa 'ö -kë wü -naa -gblüdë 'ka, 'ö wü =gban "pɛpɛ -dhɛ ö -kuu "dhiϋ : =soo- -ta -wü -nu oo-, -ta 'gu -ta -wü -nu oo-, -maa -nu oo, a n 'bha wü "pɛpɛ 'kö 'wo -kë -zë bho wü 'ka -a -nu =gban -wo kë -nu =dhiɔɔ -wo -bha. =Dhɛ 'ö -kë "dhϋ 'yö laabhölaa 'dhö dhiang sü 'yö- pö : « Ma "sɛ 'gü -mɛ -nu, -dhɛ =ya =kpaɔ ka -bha -ee ? Ka nuwɛɛ "sɛ -bha mü ? Ka nuwɛɛ ka -de gaa- yë -bha mü ? Kö 'ka =gwëë, 'ka -ya n -dhɛ "gbɩɩ- bha 'aa -yö kë ? Kö ka dhɔɔbhaa -wɔn 'ö 'dhö -Zlaan Atanna 'ö yö nü mɛ =gban kwa -zo yö- -dhɛ 'ka, kö -ya kë ka -dhɛ 'dɔɔndhö bha 'aa -yö kë ? Kö kaa- 'në -nu -wo -ya ka -dhɛ pinngdhö, kö 'mɛ 'dhɛ -nu 'ö dhe 'yaa- -nu -gɔ, kö -wo dhe -së 'sü, kö -wa 'gü 'në -së 'kpɔ, kö =sii -yö kë -a -nu 'gü bha 'aa -yö kë ?

Kö kaa- 'në 'dhɛ -nu 'ö 'wo "kwi =plöö, 'ö "kwi =plöö -dhɛ -bha -kë -a -nu -bha "gbɩɩ- -sü bha- -wɔn 'gü, 'pë 'ö kwa dë -nu 'waa- -bhö 'ö 'wo dho 'wo- -bhö, dhe 'ö kwa dë -nu 'waa zun- -bha, 'ö 'wo dho 'wo zun- -bha, -dhɛ 'ö kwa dë -nu 'waa- -ga, 'ö 'wo dho 'wo- -ga... kö biaan 'ö "dhϋ, kö -yö 'go -a -nu -bha bha 'aa -yö 'go -oo ?

Nu 'ö 'ka- wo ma =dhiɔɔ -wo -bha bha, 'ka -a kë -së -dedewo. Ka -dhɛ 'ö 'a- wo bha, a- -wo "dhϋ kö 'ka 'dho ma dhebë 'sü -dhɛ 'gü, ö dë -nu "piϋ. 'Ma- -yɔ kë 'nu 'ma n bo. -A 'sü -wɔn nü 'ö -ya 'to. 'Mɛ -nu 'ö- -dhɛ 'dhö- -bha =dhɛ -wo -dho 'to- n "piϋ yö kö yɛng- -nu 'yi yi "yan 'to 'dho -mɛ -nu -gɔ, wo -mü : 'pö- dë -nu, 'pö- dhe -nu, -kwɛɛ 'në -nu, "nɛɛ- 'në -nu waa- 'në 'sɛɛnnë -nu 'ka. =Ya 'go yö -zë -a 'gü, mɛ "pɛpɛ 'ö 'ka to, ka -dho 'dho-. N "tɔngdhe bha -a 'tɔ -mü =Geetiinë 'ka. A- -pö =Geetiinë. 'Dho 'ö kaa- wo bha, kö 'ka 'tɔ "wɛɛ pö, ka -bha 'ö kaa- -slɔɔ 'gü, kö ka -ta -wɔn -mü. -A -pö mü =dhɛ ka -dho =loo mü =dɛɛ. -A -nu "yan -yö ka -gɔ =dhɛ "gwannë -yö ö "yan -to -mɔɔ -gɔ. 'Ka 'tɔ "wɛɛ pö -wo -dho ka -ma. -A -gɛn -mü =dhɛ -wo -dho ka 'sü =dhɛ =kwan -mɛ -nu 'dhö. Kö 'ka 'dho, kö kaa- "ta -yö dhi bha 'aa -yö kë -oo ? » 'Yö 'wo- pö : « -A 'mii -na »

=Dhɛ 'ö- -nu =gban 'wo wo bo pë -bhö -sü 'ka =dhɛ -kɔ bha- 'dhö, 'yö 'wo dho "tan bha- 'ka 'wo =loo- 'ka 'pö- bha- 'gü. -A pö -sü nü 'ö =Geetiinë, kö dhebë bha -waa nu- -nu -dhɛ, =wa nu- 'ka -gblüdë Laabhölaa -dhɛ. <h>3. Dhebë 'në do 'bha 'ö ö bha 'në dha 'ö-wo "siϋ gɔn -ziisü -gɔ -Mɔɔsii “sɛ 'gü</h>

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do 'ka -Mɔɔsii "sɛ 'gü, 'pödhɛ do 'bha 'ö 'wo- -dhɛ Bangfoodha -a 'gü, 'yö -Mɔɔsii dhebë do 'bha bha, 'ö -suö dhia" "piϋ 'ö dho "yi =bhaa. -Yö -to "yi =bhaa mü 'yö "siϋ 'dhö -da -a -bha 'kɔ dhee" 'ka -a ziaan 'gü. 'Në bha -a dë waa- gɔɔn- 'gbɛ -wo -gun "kpɛnngdhö mü, "kɛɛ mɛ 'bha -kɔ 'yii kë =mɔɔ -da 'kɔ bha- 'gü -sü -bha, "siϋ nɛɛ- 'ö gun 'kɔ -bha -a "dhi -bha bha -a -wɔn 'gü. "Yi 'në -nu 'kö 'wo gun 'kɔ "wɛɛ -nu 'gü, -wo kë- -nu =gban -wɛnng "siϋ bha- -bha, "kɛɛ 'yii 'wɔn 'bha -yan. "Yi =bhaa -dhɛ =de 'pö -a -bha -kë =gblɛɛn -sü bha- -wɔn 'gü, mɛ 'bha faan 'yii kë dɔ -dho "yi 'sü- -dhɛ 'gü. Woo- kë =dhɛ ? =Klingkling =ya yö- -nu -ta. -Yö -to yö nü- 'gü, 'yö dhebë 'në bha 'ö nu.

-A =loo -sü nü "gbɩɩ-, kö =ya ö kwaa- ö bha "gbʋnggbʋ 'ö gun- =gwinng- -a -zü "siaa- ; 'yö pö yöö -sɔ 'kɔ bha- 'gü, kö 'ö ö bha 'në bha 'sü, "kɛɛ 'yö mɛ -nu 'wo- kun, -a pö -sü 'ka- -dhɛ =dhɛ 'ya 'dho ö -de zë-. 'Wɔn 'ö bha 'yö mɛ =gban "dhi dɔ bong 'ka.

<h>4. Ziaan 'ö dho =naɔ -bha -yö =gblɛɛn "wɛ -ee ?</h>

'Nëglɔɔn 'në do 'bha nü 'sëëbho -dhɛ =kpaɔyi do 'ka, 'yö- pö -Zlaan -dhɛ ö bha 'sëë -wo 'gü : « Atanna -Zlaan, -a kë kö =naɔ -yö nu n -gɔ 'kɔɔdhö, kö 'a kë =naɔ -mɛ 'ka -dhe ! » =Dhɛ 'ö -ya bhɛa" bha- wo =dhɛ -kɔ bha- 'dhö, 'ö "tϋng kpö 'në 'bha =ya ziö, 'yö dho "kwi =plöö, ö bha mɛ -nu =tuaabho kë -dhɛ 'gü. =Dhɛkpaɔyi do 'ka mü, 'yö gun ö bha ziaan ziö sië, 'yö -kpan =gbëë 'në sɛɛnnë do "dhi "pu -sü -bha -kpinng -ta kö 'wëë- "dhɛ -ya pa -sü 'ka "wɛ "sɛnngdhö =dhɛ mɛ -yö -më -kë. 'Yö 'gbaannu 'yö 'wëë- bha- -ga zuudhö. 'Yö -dhɛ -ga ö -züzü, 'yö 'yii mɛ 'bha yö. 'Yö pö yöö ö -kɔ -da 'gü, "kɛɛ 'yö ö -zo gɔn, 'yö- pö ö -de -dhɛ : « 'Wëë- ya 'a ü 'sü, "iin 'a ü kë 'mü =dhɛ -oo ? A- -pö =tɔn -Zlaan -dhɛ =naɔ -yö nu n -gɔ 'kɔɔdhö, "kɛɛ -a 'dhɛ 'kö ya, -yö -kpinng -ta -wa ! -Kë =dhɛ -wɔn =nɛ -oo ? 'A 'dho ü 'ka =tɔn 'kɔɔdhö -ee ? » 'Yö ö -zo 'bha gɔn, 'yö 'wëë- bha- to 'yö dho.

=Dhɛkpaɔyi "wɛɛ 'bha 'ka kö =ya ö yeekë =ya 'dho 'pödhö, 'yö gun =niëë sië "ka "flɩɩ- -dhɛ 'bha 'ö gun 'pö- "sɔɔ mü, -a 'gü. 'Ö dho -dhɛ -ga gwɛ -dhü do 'bha 'ö gun bha- =wlöö, kö gbɔ 'kpii- do 'ö- "dhi 'dhö "pʋ -sü 'ka, -yö mü, kö "sënng -ya pa -sü 'ka "wɛ "sɛnngdhö. 'Yö pö ö -de -dhɛ : « =Naɔ -dede =nɛ, "kɛɛ 'yaa n -gɔ =tɔn 'kɔɔdhö -wa n dë -nuu ! »

Kö =ya 'gbaannu =dhɛ "dhü 'ö 'wo- gban -a 'dhö, -ya -ga sië, kö- zuëga -yö 'zëë- zë kë sië ; kö 'pë 'ö ziö sië- -gɔ 'gü =dhɛ -zogɔndhe 'dhö, -Zlaan nü ö bha pë dɔ. "Kɛɛ 'yö- to 'ö ö bha 'dho wo. =Dhɛ 'ö =loo "kwanngdhö, 'yö -kpan ö "tɛɛdo do 'bha bha, -a -bha, 'yö- pö- -dhɛ =dhɛ 'ya -kpan "sënng -bha, "kɛɛ -a 'sü -dhɔ 'yii kë ö kë. -Yö gbɔ 'gü gwɛ -dhü =wlöö "ka "flɩɩ- -dhɛ 'gü. 'Yö- 'tɔngdë 'ö pö- -dhɛ : « Bhi -zë slaa" nü ü 'gü. 'Ü -kpan "sënng -bha 'yö 'bhaa- 'sü 'kö =dhɛ ? -A "bin ! Ü -ta -yö -ma -sü 'ka -dedewo. »

Dhiang bha -go -a "dhi -sü nü 'ö "gbɩɩ- kö -ya ziö =dhɛ =saaga -yö -ziö =ya 'dho mü. -dedewo 'yö dho 'yö -kpan gbɔ bha- -bha kö -yö mü "dhϋ tɛan- 'ka, "kɛɛ kö -a -te "dhiϋ -ya "dhiϋ. 'Yö- bho- "dhiϋ. 'Ö dho -dhɛ -ga kö =mlɛɛ bhɛ -zizisü nü 'ö -ya ö "klϋ kë gbɔ bha- 'gü ya. 'Yö gbɔ bha- -te "dhiϋ yö- "dhiϋ "lɛɛdhö -deewo, 'yö dho 'ö "mlüü -kë 'yö gbɔ bha -a sü "lɛɛdhö 'ö- dɔ ö =gwinng- kö 'ö 'dho 'ö- -zuö ö "tɔngdë bha- -ta 'kɔɔdhö. -A -bha 'gü -a "tɔngdë -yö =sua nü- -kë ö -gɔ ; -a -wɔn 'gü, 'yö- "piϋ =dhɛ 'ö ö mlɔɔ bho- -gɔ. =Dhɛ 'kö =loo 'kɔ "dhi -bha, 'ö ö "yan -zë -a -kpan ö "tɔngdë bha- -bha 'kɔɔdhö, dɔ nü 'ö- wo "kpɛnngdhö 'ö gbɔ bha- -zuö -a -ta 'kɔɔdhö 'mü kö -ya ziö -biang 'ka =dhɛ =saaga -yö -ziö. Gbɔ bha -a -pö "siaa- -sü nü 'ö "gbɩɩ- kö =mlɛɛ 'ö gun 'nu -a 'gü "dhϋ bha, =ya "gla "sënng 'gü -deewo =ya =loo "siaa-.

=Naɔ -dede =ya nu =tɔn -a -gɔ 'kɔɔdhö.

=Naɔ 'ö gɔndë 'në bha 'ö kë- -dhɛ -Zlaan -gɔ bha, -a 'gü -wɔn -yö kë -kë =dhɛ -kɔ bha- 'dhö.

Ö "tϋng 'ö kë- to ö -dega -zë -dhiang 'gü bha, -a -ga 'ö- 'gü -wɔn -së 'ö -kë -a -dhɛ bha.

-Yö kë ö zuë" -kë -sɛa 'güdandhe -nu bha, -a -nu 'gü, 'ö -Zlaan dhɔɔbhaa 'ö -kë =dhɛ -kɔ 'ö yöö -dede 'ö kë- pö 'ka -Zlaan -dhɛ bha- 'dhö.

'Wɔn yaa 'ö- "tɔngdë 'ö kë- -ya ö zuë" "piϋ 'ö- kë 'nu- 'ka bha, -yö kë -gla -a -gɔ 'wɔn -së 'gü.

Ziaan 'ö dho =naɔ -bha -yö =gblɛɛn. Zuë" -sɛamɛ nü 'ö =mɔɔ- 'sü -sü -bha, 'yö- =trɔɔn =slɔɔ.

=Ya 'go mü, 'mɛ 'ö 'bha pö bhii 'wɔn 'bha kë, kö ü zuëga -yö 'zëëzë kö -a kë -sü 'gü, -yö -së kö 'bha 'dho- kë-. -A 'gbɛ -dhɛ 'gü 'yaa dhi mɛ -gɔ. "Kɛɛ ü zuëga -zë 'yii 'zëë- zë kë, kö -a kë -sü -yö ü zuë" =niida, -a kë. -A "dhiϋ ta 'gbɛ -dhɛ -yö -dhi mɛ -gɔ.
﻿
<h>5. =Gee do 'bha -bha dhebë 'në do 'bha 'kun 'ö- wo 'nʋbë 'ka</h>

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do 'ka, yö =gee 'ö 'wo- -dhɛ 'mamɔɔnë, "iin 'zü "siϋ dhuu" -gee bha 'ö yö "kpɛnng. -A -bha pë -mü "siϋ dhuu" -sü 'ka dhebë -nu -gɔ zuëën- 'gü, 'ö sü 'yënng- -kë "gbɩɩ- "tϋng -bha, blɛɛ" yi 'ka ; kë "dhϋ kö "tɛɛ 'ya 'dho 'dho- pɛng -klaan -nu 'ka, 'ö 'wo 'pö- -gϋ. =Gee bha =ya yö "kpɛnng =dhɛ -kɔ bha- 'dhö, 'yö dhebë -nu =wa ziö- -gɔ -bɛng 'ka. -A -ga, yö 'ö- wo "kpɛnng bha, 'yö kpa dhebë 'në do 'bha bha- =keng-. Dhebë 'në bha, =loo 'ö- wo "wlëëdhɛ 'bha bha- 'gü bha, 'yö- -gɛn 'dhö -da wöng 'gü, 'yö -pö, kö -foo -nu =gban -yaa zë. -Yö -to 'waannu -sü 'ka -dhɛ bha- 'gü, 'yö =gee bha 'ö nu. Kö ü- -kë mü =dhɛ, 'bhii -a kë 'mü =dhɛ -ee, -a -gɛn 'yii kë -da pë 'bha 'gü, "kɛɛ -gblu, yöö =de 'pö -ya -pö, "kɛɛ dhebë 'në bha -a "sɔɔ -dhɛ -dede 'gü mü. Wɛng -wa -wɔ wo 'ko "dhiϋ mü. -Yö -to dhebë 'në "sɔɔ mü 'yö- pö- -dhɛ : « Mɛ -së, ü -dhɔ =ya n kë "gbɩɩ- -wa. Ü -dhɔ 'ö -bhɔ n kë -sü 'ka, -a yi -ya =gwëë, "kɛɛ maa -a kë 'nu -kɔ 'ö- 'gü, 'maa gun -a -kɔ yö -sü 'ka. -A -kë "dhϋ -sü bha- 'gü, -yö n "piϋ =dhɛ kwɛng 'ko kë -mlɛɛ 'gü. Dɔ "gbɩɩ- 'yɔn -mɛ dhe, n dhɔɔbhaa ».

'Wɔn bha -yö kë -kë =dhɛ -gwëmɛ -yö ö "yan to wɛngga -gɔ.

=Dhɛ 'ö =gee bha 'ö- pö "dhϋ, 'yö dhebë 'në bha 'ö- pö : « 'Yö n dë -bha =gee, 'wɔn 'kö bha -yö "dhϋ 'yö 'bhaa- pö 'nu n -dhɛ "vaandhö, 'yö kwɛng =plɛ 'ko sëë "suma bho ya -ee ? 'Yaa "gbɩɩ-, 'wɔn 'ü- pö bha 'ma- ma. -Siö mɛ -dhɛ -wɔn 'yaa kë "dhϋ».

'Kwa- pö "dhϋ, kö kwa- -pö =dhɛ tɛan- -wɔn pö -sü 'ö "vaandhö 'wɔn -nu 'gü, wo 'ko nu -dhɛ bha, 'yö -së. 'Bha 'dho ü kwaa- ü këyɔɔ -zü 'ö sëëbho kö -blɛɛsü kö 'ü gun -naa tɛan- -wɔn pö- -dhɛ =taama. -A -kë "dhϋ -sü 'yaa -së.

    
    
    
﻿
<h>6. -Kɔ 'ö -kë -a -bha 'ö 'wo "Maadhɛ -dhɛ "Maadhö</h>

'Ö gun "tϋng 'bha 'ka kö dha 'yaa ban sië, kö mɛ "bhɩɩ- -nu woo- kë -kɔ 'ö -a -bha kö 'wo dha "yi =slɔɔ Gbɛɛ" =plöö, kö- -kɔ 'bhaa 'dhö.

'Yö Gbɛɛ" =plöö -mɛ -nu 'ö- -naa "sɛ -yö -kë "Maadhɛ 'ka bha, -a -naa =dhuutii waa- ö dɔ -bha -mɛ -nu, 'wo dho -dhɛ -ma -ga. 'Ö gun kë sië "dhϋ bha, kö 'në dhebë do nü =dhuutii bha- -gɔ. -A -ga, 'yö -dɛ 'dhö- pö =dhɛ =dhuutii bha -yö ö bha 'në ga dosɛngsɛng 'ö -a -gɔ bha, -ya kë "saa- 'ka. =Ya bo -kë "dhϋ -sü 'ka dha -yö -dho ban-. "Saa- 'ö "dhϋ bha yö -mü =dhɛ -wo -yɛga do 'pɔn kö 'në 'ö "dhϋ bha, -wa 'to "bhɩɩ- 'ka kö -wa -zuö 'gü, -wo "sɛ =loo- -ta. =Dhuutii -kɔ =ya =mɔɔ -a -kë "dhϋ -sü -bha dha -yö -dho ban-, 'ö ta -pë -nu 'wo -dhi. 'Yö =dhuutii bha 'ö -wɩ -a -bha.

=Dhɛ 'ö 'wo nu 'wo =loo wo -yɛɛ =bhaa 'wii wo "dhi bho- -ta mɛ 'bha -dhɛ kö 'yii kë kë 'pö- dë -nu -kpɛa 'ö 'wo kë to -a -nu 'ka.

=Dhɛ 'ö -kë "dhϋ, 'yö 'wo dho -gblɛɛn 'kpɔ 'gü "bü =zinng 'gü 'pö- bha- "sɔɔ, 'yö -yɛ bha 'wo- pɔn. =Dhɛ 'ö 'wo wo bo, 'yö 'wo "kpënng- kpɔ 'në bha- -gɔ 'yö 'wo dho- 'ka 'ö 'wo- -ziö -yɛ ga bha 'gü, 'wo "sɛ kpa- -ta =dhɛ -kɔ 'ö 'wo- pö- 'ka -a -nu bha- 'dhö.

"Saa- bha -a bho -sü nü 'ö "gbɩɩ- kö dha 'kpikikpiki -ya -ya ban -sü -bha "siasia- mü.

-A -kë -sü bha- 'gü, 'yö 'wo- pö =dhɛ 'ö -kë =dhɛ 'në bha -wo -gun -a -dhɛ sië "Maadhe, 'ö- -gɔ =ya 'to mɛ =gbaan- 'wɔn 'gü bha, -a 'tɔ bha -wa -ya "Maadhɛ -bha.

'Pë 'ö -kë =dɛɛ 'ö 'wo "Maadhɛ -dhɛ "Maadhö bha, 'yö bha.

-Zlaan -yö -mɔɔ -a -bha 'ö bɔ mɛ doseng -ta 'ö mɛ 'gbɛ dha, "iin 'zü 'ö mɛ 'gbɛ 'gü =see.

<h>7. 'Mɛ'ö 'yaa 'dhangbho 'wɔn "dhiϋ, -ka ka kwaa- -zü kö -a "yan -yö dɔ 'wɔn 'gü</h>

"Kwi -gɔ -mɛ 'kpii- 'ö -kë mɛ tii 'ka, 'yö- pö yö -zë 'yaa 'dhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ tongtongdhö. =Ya kë "wɛ, 'yö -kë -a zë -dhiang 'ka =dhɛ, 'yaa 'dhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ. 'Mɛ 'ö 'kwa "wɩ sië- 'ka ya, -yö -gun za -gɔ "yɛ -mɛ nü- 'ka. =Ya kë "kwi -wo 'gü, 'yö 'wo- pö 'zuzö.

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do 'ka, 'yö gɔndë 'në do 'bha bha 'ö go ö -gɔ 'pödhö 'ö nu dhebë 'në do 'bha -tazɔn 'zuzë =plöö dü -wɔn "gblʋʋ "piϋ. 'Wɔn bha -yö kë sië "dhϋ Dannëngdhö. =Dhɛ 'ö -kë "dhϋ, 'yö 'wo zadɔ -yi -ya -a -nu -gɔ. =Dhɛkpaɔyi bha, mɛ "bhɩɩdhe nu 'ö- wo, -yö -gun -ziisü. =Dhɛ 'ö 'wo- -nu dhɛa" kpɔ, 'yö mɛ -tazɔn -mɛ bha 'ö -ziö ö -wo 'gü =dhɛ dhebë 'në bha nü ö bha 'në zë dü 'gü ; 'yö 'zuzö mi bha 'ö dhe "gbʋʋ- 'në bha- dhɛa" kpɔ 'ö- pö : « =Dhaviɛɛyö, dü -wɔn 'ö 'wo -ya ü -bha ya -yö "dhϋ tɛan- 'ka -ee ? Tɛan- -mü =dhɛ dü ü -gɔ -ee ? » Dhebë 'në bha 'yii kë- dɔ bhiëë" =gblɛɛn -bha, -a pö nü 'ö- wo =ii. =Dhɛ 'ö- pö "dhϋ, 'yö 'zuzö mi bha 'ö- pö- -dhɛ : « =Dhaviɛɛyö, -a -zɔn mɛ =gban "yaan 'ka yö =dhɛ dü -yö ö -gɔ. »

'Yö dhebë 'në bha 'ö- pö -wo yö "kpɛnng. 'Yö mɛ =gban 'dhö go 'kɔɔdhö 'yö 'wo nu 'dhuëng- -ta zadɔ 'gü -kɔ bha- "dhiϋ mü. 'Yö dhe "gbʋʋ- 'në bha, 'ö pö -wo 'dho -tɔ klëën do 'dhɔ- kö -wo nu- 'ka. "Vaandhö "wɛ =ni, kö 'pë bha -wa nu- 'ka. 'Yö- pö -wa "dhi kë "bϋwɛ, 'yö 'wo- -kë "dhϋ.

Mɛ =gban "pɛpɛ "yan "dhiϋ mü bha, 'yö dhebë 'në bha 'ö ö -gɔ -sɔ 'pë bha- 'gü, 'yö ö =sɔɔ "sɔɔ -kë, 'yö ö =sɔɔ "sɔɔ -kë, 'yö ö =sɔɔ "sɔɔ -kë, 'yö- -dhɛ =gban "pɛpɛ 'ö ma -tɔ klëën bha- 'gü mü. Kö mɛ =gbaan =wa -ya kwɛɛ" 'kun -sü -bha. =Dhɛ 'ö -kë "dhϋ, 'yö pö -wo sɔ kpa ö -ta, 'yö 'wo- kpa- -ta. 'Wo dho "kan- wo -ta, kö -tɔ klëën bha, -ya -ya -pa ö diëë -sü -bha. Kö -yö =glüü "glüü kë sië 'ö go- 'ka "siaa-. 'Yö 'zuzö mi bha 'ö 'dhangbho 'wɔn bha- "dhiϋ, 'yö pö : « =Dhaviɛɛyö -yö 'to "dhϋ. » =Sua 'ö 'zuzö mi bha 'ö- -kë, -yö -kë =dhɛ mɛ -ya pö =dhaviɛɛyö -bhö 'dho- -bha 'bha wo. Pë do 'ö- dɔ -ziaawo -a 'gü, -yö -gun "gbɩɩ-. -Yö -kë =dhɛ "flʋkpongdhe -yö -ziö. -Tɔ klëën waa- dhebë 'në 'ö bha 'dho 'ö 'wo- 'wo dhang- 'gü 'yi bha -yi bha 'ka, nü 'ö 'kwa -a -bha dɔ wo =dɛɛ ya. -Waa mɔɔ- -a -gɔ 'pödhö, -waa mɔɔ- -dhɛ =gban 'gü, 'wii -kpan -a -bha 'ö nu 'ö yö- 'ka =dɛɛ -bha.

Za 'dhɛ 'ö bha -a "dhiϋ -ya -dhɛ -yö kë -kë =dhɛ -kɔ bha- 'dhö.

-Yö -sü yi bha nü- -bha, 'yö 'zuzö mi bha 'ö 'dhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ.

'Mɛ 'ö -yaa pö 'yaa 'dhangbho 'wɔn 'ö "dhiϋ, -ka 'wɔn -zɔn -a -dhɛ kö- "yan -yö dɔ- 'gü.
﻿
<h>7. 'Mɛ'ö 'yaa 'dhangbho 'wɔn "dhiϋ, -ka ka kwaa- -zü kö -a "yan -yö dɔ 'wɔn 'gü</h>

"Kwi -gɔ -mɛ 'kpii- 'ö -kë mɛ tii 'ka, 'yö- pö yö -zë 'yaa 'dhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ tongtongdhö. =Ya kë "wɛ, 'yö -kë -a zë -dhiang 'ka =dhɛ, 'yaa 'dhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ. 'Mɛ 'ö 'kwa "wɩ sië- 'ka ya, -yö -gun za -gɔ "yɛ -mɛ nü- 'ka. =Ya kë "kwi -wo 'gü, 'yö 'wo- pö 'zuzö.

'Yö dhebë 'në bha 'ö- pö -wo yö "kpɛnng. 'Yö mɛ =gban 'dhö go 'kɔɔdhö 'yö 'wo nu 'dhuëng- -ta zadɔ 'gü -kɔ bha- "dhiϋ mü. 'Yö dhe "gbʋʋ- 'në bha, 'ö pö -wo 'dho -tɔ klëën do 'dhɔ- kö -wo nu- 'ka. "Vaandhö "wɛ =ni, kö 'pë bha -wa nu- 'ka. 'Yö- pö -wa "dhi kë "bϋwɛ, 'yö 'wo- -kë "dhϋ.

Kö mɛ =gbaan =wa -ya kwɛɛ" 'kun -sü -bha. =Dhɛ 'ö -kë "dhϋ, 'yö pö -wo sɔ kpa ö -ta, 'yö 'wo- kpa- -ta. 'Wo dho "kan- wo -ta, kö -tɔ klëën bha, -ya -ya -pa ö diëë -sü -bha. Kö -yö =glüü "glüü kë sië 'ö go- 'ka "siaa-. 'Yö 'zuzö mi bha 'ö 'dhangbho 'wɔn bha- "dhiϋ, 'yö pö : « =Dhaviɛɛyö -yö 'to "dhϋ. » =Sua 'ö 'zuzö mi bha 'ö- -kë, -yö -kë =dhɛ mɛ -ya pö =dhaviɛɛyö -bhö 'dho- -bha 'bha wo. Pë do 'ö- dɔ -ziaawo -a 'gü, -yö -gun "gbɩɩ-. -Yö -kë =dhɛ "flʋkpongdhe -yö -ziö. -Tɔ klëën waa- dhebë 'në 'ö bha 'dho 'ö 'wo- 'wo dhang- 'gü 'yi bha -yi bha 'ka, nü 'ö 'kwa -a -bha dɔ wo =dɛɛ ya. -Waa mɔɔ- -a -gɔ 'pödhö, -waa mɔɔ- -dhɛ =gban 'gü, 'wii -kpan -a -bha 'ö nu 'ö yö- 'ka =dɛɛ -bha.

-Yö -sü yi bha nü- -bha, 'yö 'zuzö mi bha 'ö 'dhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ.
